Current Commentary

Opening of the Pan-American Peace Conference 64

— Lang

The Pan-American Peace Conference opened yesterday in the capital of Argentina. At a time when aggressors around the world are united in attacking the god of peace, it is a welcome development that the twenty-one countries of the Americas can come together in the halls of peace to discuss the organization of peace in the Western Hemisphere.

This Pan-American Peace Conference was initiated and convened by US President Roosevelt at the end of January this year. Therefore, at the opening ceremony, this re-elected "master of the White House" did not hesitate to travel there in person to attend. Why did President Roosevelt convene this peace conference and attach so much importance to it? Simply put, the convocation of this conference lies in promoting the United States' Good Neighbor Policy and selling commercial reciprocity agreements. We know that the United States' policy towards Latin America was previously to adhere to the narrow definition of the Monroe Doctrine. The strict implementation of this aggressive Monroe Doctrine only aroused anti-American sentiment in the small countries. Therefore, by the time of President Roosevelt, this "big stick diplomacy" was abandoned and a gentle Good Neighbor Policy was adopted instead. Behind this Good Neighbor Policy, there is naturally a demand for the outward development of financial power. This can be seen by looking at Secretary of State Hull's visit to South America with commercial reciprocity agreements for sale.

Regardless of the underlying motives of the United States in convening this peace conference, if we look at the peace conference itself, it is of great help to the promotion of the international peace movement. Because the main issue discussed at this conference is how to promote the peace organization of the Americas. In the past, the United States had signed four kinds of peace treaties, but none of them had the participation of a large number of countries, so their power was not great. At this conference, representatives of various countries will certainly further discuss how to enhance the power of these peace treaties. It may even go further and organize a League of Nations for the Americas. This kind of peaceful effort will naturally help promote the entire international peace.

Many people believe that the opening of the Pan-American Peace Conference will take an adversarial stance against the League of Nations in Geneva. In fact, this is not very accurate. Because Roosevelt's foreign policy contains a very strong tendency towards international cooperation. The history of the past four years is a good example. On the contrary, the further cooperation of the countries of the Americas can make the United States' relationship with Geneva closer through the wooing of the small countries of South America. Moreover, the regional security system is actually the beginning of the entire collective security system. Therefore, the Pan-American Peace Conference is of great significance to the promotion of the international peace movement.

The cooperation of the countries of the Americas not only has a great impact on international peace, but also has a significant relationship to the development of the situation in the Far East. We know that President Roosevelt has been vigorously implementing a policy of giant ships and big guns in recent years. Behind this policy of giant ships and big guns is the development of the situation in the Western Pacific. But before implementing countermeasures against the aggressors in the Far East, the relations between the countries of the Americas must first be adjusted. And the convocation of this Pan-American Conference actually contains this important significance of uniting the internal affairs.

Fierce Rebel Offensive on Madrid, Germany and Russia Still Supplying Both Sides, League of Nations to Meet on the 10th of This Month 65

Madrid: The Nationalist forces launched a fierce offensive this morning, seemingly determined to break through the capital's defenses. Intense fighting is currently underway on the Madrid front, with the intensity of artillery fire unprecedented in a month. (1st Reuters)

(London) This agency has just received a cable from Spain confirming the news carried in the News Chronicle, stating that 5,000 Germans were spotted landing at ports held by the Spanish Nationalist forces. Whether these individuals are German soldiers, whether they are carrying weapons, or whether they are wearing uniforms has not yet been determined. Officials here have stated that if these Germans are indeed carrying weapons or are German soldiers, the British government will undoubtedly express its regret if this is proven to be true. While individual enlistment in the Spanish army may not violate the non-intervention agreement, soldiers enlisting in another country requires the permission of their home government, which would be a blatant violation of the non-intervention agreement. (1st Havas)

Gibraltar: According to reliable sources, a Russian general and 100 officers arrived in Malaga today, and the local militia is now under their command. Twenty aircraft, believed to be of Soviet origin, will be delivered to the port this week. (3rd Reuters)

Gibraltar: A person from Seville declared today that 5,000 Germans wearing Spanish Falangist uniforms arrived in Seville on Saturday. In addition, 30 Italian tanks are being transported to the Malaga front. (30th National Telegram)

(London) At the request of the Spanish government, the Council of the League of Nations has decided to hold a meeting in Geneva on the 10th of this month. The British chief representative will be Foreign Secretary Eden himself. This morning, sources claimed that the British government has received reports from various sources that between 2,000 and 7,000 Germans have recently arrived in the Seville area. If these Germans are a military organization or carrying weapons, the British government will express its deep regret. However, reports received indicate that they appear to be German volunteers. British concerns about the Spanish Civil War have increased considerably. However, one thing that Britain is also paying attention to is that a large number of German volunteers are also entering Spain from time to time. (1st Reuters)

(Geneva) Today, various circles here are extremely apprehensive about Spain's request for the Council of the League of Nations to convene a special meeting. The absence of Germany and Italy will make any public discussion a one-sided action without any practical effect. It is feared that the actions of the Council will not be superior to the work of the Non-Intervention Committee. Many believe that Spanish Foreign Minister Del Vayo may rely on the assistance of the Soviet government to propose blockading the ports held by the Nationalist forces and cutting off their supplies. However, any suggestion will be ignored by the public. (1st Reuters)

(London) It is rumored that the British government has notified the Secretariat of the League of Nations that it would be futile for the Council to hold a meeting now to discuss the situation in Spain. This statement was explicitly denied by officials. Foreign Secretary Eden had talks with French Ambassador Corbin and Chilean Ambassador Edwards (the chairman of the current session of the Council) to discuss the convening of the Council meeting. Political circles believe that Germany and Italy will refuse to participate, so the Council meeting will not be of any significance. After the meeting of the Council, it will be declared that the Spanish Civil War must be limited in scope to prevent its expansion, and that the principle of "limiting the scope" can be implemented by the Adjustment Committee of the Non-Intervention Method. (30th Havas)

US-French War Debt Settlement Agreed Upon 68

(Paris) It was learned today that France owes a total of 1,200,000,000,000 francs in war debts to the United States. According to the payment method now agreed upon, 600,000,000,000 francs will be paid annually, to be paid off in twenty years. (1st National Telegram)

(Paris) It is said today by authoritative sources here that the United States and France have decided to clear up the entire war debt issue. The United States Ambassador to France, Bullitt, met with French Foreign Minister Delbos for a long time, and a principle agreement was reached. Details will be discussed later. It is likely that the United States and France will agree that the war debts owed by France will be re-evaluated and then paid off in installments within twenty years. However, the British war debts must also be resolved at the same time, so that it can be used as a result of the three-nation monetary agreement, and can be regarded as a sign of respect for the treaty. French Prime Minister Blum has notified Bullitt that France is prepared to negotiate quickly and does not intend to argue much, and does not intend to make any demands on the United States. However, this measure is limited to the three countries of Britain, France, and the United States, and has nothing to do with other debtor countries such as Italy. According to estimates, France currently owes the United States a total of 400 million US dollars in principal and interest, and Britain owes even more than this amount. The last time France made a payment was in 1931, and Britain in 1933, but they have paid a small amount since then to show their commitment. France also hopes that the war debt agreement can be integrated with other political and economic agreements, so that world peace can be consolidated and international trade restored by abolishing import quotas and reducing rates. Since Britain's debts are greater than France's, France will also handle the settlement with Britain after the settlement. The United States and France will first discuss the total amount of debt and then discuss the payment method. Prime Minister Blum may personally go to Washington to discuss this matter, but the United States must first acknowledge that France has not defaulted. As for the total amount of debt in the future, it will be lower than before the default, but it will not be merely a token payment. According to the original agreement, France has defaulted on 21.5 million US dollars, and the total amount of principal and interest will reach 650 million US dollars by 1987. Here, the talks between the United States and France are still being kept strictly confidential today, and even the Foreign Ministry denies that the US Ambassador has met with the French Foreign Minister. (30th National Telegram)

Li Ziziluosi Again Delivers a Speech: Developing Sino-British Trade; My Income Tax Collection Should Be Fair; Foreign Nationals Should Voluntarily Pay 72

(London) Sir Richard Leith-Ross, the British government's chief economic advisor, delivered a speech at the China Association's annual banquet tonight, detailing China's economic situation and Sino-British trade relations. The annual banquet was chaired by Conservative Member of Parliament Lord Winterton, and the attendance was unprecedented in recent years. Important guests included Guo Taiqi, the Chinese Ambassador to the UK, Koupbert Lieck, the new resident representative of the Export Credits Guarantee Department in China, Conservative Member of Parliament Mallin, former Ambassador to China Sir Cadogan, Barclays Bank Vice-Chairman and Export Credits Guarantee Department Executive Committee Member Sir Caulcutt, Lord Cantelupe, a member of the House of Lords, and Lord Yarnis, General Manager of the General Insurance Company. In his speech, Li first described the smooth implementation of China's new currency system and recalled that China had paper money circulating throughout the country as early as the Yuan Dynasty. Regarding the Chinese government's proposed income tax, Li believed that the government must first provide a fair and perfect guarantee for the collection of the tax, and then foreign nationals in China could comply. However, British merchants should not insist on giving up the tax exemptions they originally enjoyed and must consider China's financial needs in a constructive spirit. Li reiterated that due to the current increase in trade and indirect tax revenue, recovery would be achieved sooner if tariffs could be modified. China's development is now extremely rapid, and the Chinese government should prioritize essential plans and implement them first, deferring less critical matters to a later date. Li also advocated that the Chinese government should make full use of foreign advisors, hoping that the foreign staff of the Salt Inspectorate would not be reduced, and that more foreigners should be hired in other government agencies. For example, if the assessment and collection of income tax were entrusted to foreign personnel, foreign nationals would be more willing to accept it. Regarding the grandeur of China's railway construction plans and the development of various public utilities, the United Kingdom should provide the necessary equipment at any time. He deeply understood that British industry, commerce, and banking circles could have close cooperation and hoped that there would also be the closest cooperation with China, agreeing to the greatest financial support for various large-scale projects. The British should also prepare to assist China in reorganizing various undertakings that are beneficial to both China and the United Kingdom. Li also stated that British industrialists should send younger and more capable personnel to China to seek further development of their businesses. Li concluded, "In the next ten years, the main task of the British in China will be to supply China with railways, electrical machinery, and other large-scale machinery needed for modern life. Therefore, the British people should have a broad vision for the ever-changing situation in the vast region of the Far East." (Reuters, 30th)

Austria Refuses to Join the German-Japanese Pact; However, Hungary Advocates Joining 73

(Vienna) Austrian Chancellor Dr. Schuschnigg met with Hungarian Prime Minister Dr. Darányi and Foreign Minister Kánya today and stated that Austria refused to join the German-Japanese Anti-Comintern Pact. Darányi proposed that Austria and Hungary jointly join the anti-communist group, to which Schuschnigg replied in this way, citing two reasons: (1) Austria learned that the German-Japanese pact was viewed by Western Europe as unhelpful to peace, so Austria did not want to provoke negative feelings from Britain and France towards Austria. (2) There is no real danger of communism in Austria. The Austrian government feels that the loyalty and assistance of the country's military and police are sufficient to deal with any attempts to disrupt peace. (Reuters, 30th)

Japanese Army Pamphlet Admits Japanese Army Is Not a Match for Russia; Insufficient Troops, Striving for Remediation; Air Force Dominates Future Wars 74

(Tokyo) The Army Ministry recently published a pamphlet, the contents of which are quite important. It is briefly described as follows: Although the Japanese military's strength is extremely superior in spirit and essence, it pales in comparison to the Soviet Far Eastern Red Army in terms of numbers. From a military strategic standpoint, the most dangerous fact is that the Japanese troops stationed in "Manchukuo" are too few. In any case, the Japanese army must maintain a similar balance with the Soviet Union's peacetime troops stationed in the Far East. One chapter in the pamphlet discusses the minimum limits of national defense strength, stating that, in view of the military strength of the Soviet Union and China, it can be seen that Japan's military preparations on the mainland are extremely incomplete. In order to avoid war and maintain Japan's lifeline on the mainland, the reorganization of military preparations is an urgent matter. The military strength required by a country must be determined by its peacetime policies, the country's current situation, and its relationship with other countries. If the military strength that the Soviet Union can place on the battlefield is as strong as various countries speculate, then Japan's current military strength, no matter how well-trained, strategically superior, or disciplined, will not be able to compensate for its insufficient numbers. It must be noted that mechanical and scientific equipment will become increasingly important in future wars. The Soviet Far Eastern military force consists of a total of fifteen divisions in peacetime, with 1,000 aircraft divided into more than 100 teams, and about 1,000 tanks. In addition, the Soviet Union has built extremely strong fortresses in the border areas, posing a constant threat of aggression to neighboring "Manchukuo." Looking back at Japan's military strength in Manchuria, what is it like? In terms of numbers, it is only one-third or one-quarter of that of the Soviet Union. As for aircraft and tanks, it is even far from comparable to the Soviet Union. Japan relies on this weak military force to patrol a meandering 3,000-mile border, maintain peace and order in an area equal to the territory of Germany and France, and guard a railway line exceeding 6,000 miles in length. The Soviet troops stationed along the Russo-Manchurian border are a strategic district garrison, while the scattered distribution of the Japanese army is a phenomenon of insufficient allocation. In short, the Japanese troops stationed in Manchuria and Korea must have sufficient strength to guard the border, maintain public order, and patrol the railway line in peacetime. In wartime, they must also resist enemy invasion. It must be known that the outcome of the initial battles along the border will have a serious impact on the entire war situation. In order to consolidate border defenses, the Russo-Manchurian border troops must have sufficient defense capabilities. In order to consolidate the defense of the Asian continent and to ensure that the first line has complete protection in the event of a war with the Soviet Union, it is necessary for the Japanese garrison to increase proportionally to the Soviet military strength.

In a possible future war, large enemy aircraft will attempt to carry out air raids on Tokyo and Japan's major military and munitions bases immediately after the outbreak of the war. If Japan lacks the ability to carry out these air raids at the beginning, it will inevitably end in a tragic defeat. Therefore, in addition to the army, Japan's air force must also be actively expanded.

The importance of the air force in modern warfare is obvious and does not need to be elaborated. However, it is also a major element in preventing war. The British naval power is far above that of Italy, but its Mediterranean fleet does not dare to deal with the Italian fleet by extreme means because Italy's air force exceeds that of Britain. From this point of view, the replenishment of the Japanese air force is indeed an urgent matter.

Finally, it also mentions the need to revitalize national administration, saying that if domestic administration is on the right track, Japan will be able to compete with the Soviet Union in military preparations. The pamphlet contains many photos of Soviet aircraft, parachutes, and tanks, and includes a map detailing important military districts in the Far East. (Reuters News)

London Fire! Crystal Palace Reduced to Ashes; Sparks Spreading During Concert; Radio Transmission Station Also Destroyed 80

While a concert was being held in the Crystal Palace tonight, there was a sudden accident, and the fire spread very quickly, reducing the entire building to ashes. The actual loss cannot be estimated. The radio transmission machine, the world's newest type, which had recently been installed in the palace, was also completely destroyed, worth tens of thousands of pounds. Less than 20 minutes after the fire started, the central part of the building was completely engulfed in flames, and the sound of it collapsing could be heard a mile away.

At 7:30 tonight, while singing was in progress, a female staff member of the palace suddenly told the musicians that there was a fire in the palace, but there was no danger. Unexpectedly, five minutes later, the fire had penetrated into the room, and the orchestra hurriedly fled for their lives, narrowly escaping the inferno. Fire brigades from all over heard the alarm and rushed to the scene to help put out the fire. There were many spectators from all directions, causing traffic congestion. The flames shot high into the sky, and the red light illuminated the sky. Members of Parliament in the House of Commons eight miles away gathered on the balcony to watch.

Four hours after the alarm was raised, at 11:15, there were three loud explosions, which shook the surrounding area. At that time, everyone was concerned about the safety of the North Tower on the edge of the railway, and all trains were stopped. Almost all of the city's fire engines were mobilized. When the fire was at its fiercest, several filmmakers drove a plane close to the fire scene, moving in and out of the sky full of flying sparks to capture the scene. Their courageous spirit amazed the onlookers. At one point, the nose of the plane was clearly tilted straight down, threatening to fall into the inferno, but with a turn, it was safe again. The audience's hair stood on end. The members of the orchestra were frustrated because their precious instruments were lost in the fire, but they were extremely fortunate to have saved their lives, because a few seconds after they ran out, the front of the palace collapsed onto the road, burying many cars parked on the side of the road. The danger was indeed imminent.

The police ordered residents around the palace to leave their homes to prevent danger. Pedestrians half a mile away felt uneasy from the heat of the fire, not to mention the firefighters stationed on the roofs and ladders of nearby buildings, so they had to change shifts in a short time. The fact that the glass was melted into a liquid by the fire also showed the intensity of the heat. At present, the North and South Towers still stand tall, but the entire building has been reduced to ashes. (Reuters, 30th)

(London) A major fire occurred here last night, and the Crystal Palace was destroyed by fire. The flames reached a height of 600 feet, and there were more than 100,000 spectators. 350 firefighters worked hard to put out the fire. The fire alarm was raised at 8:30 in the evening, and all fire engines were dispatched. It was not extinguished until after midnight. Tens of thousands of gallons of water were poured. Only two towers remain. The loss is estimated at around £200,000. It is currently difficult to determine whether the radio transmission station in the tower can be preserved. The glass roof of the central grand circular hall collapsed when the fire was fierce, and ashes flew two miles away. (Guomin Electric, 30th)

(London) After the famous Crystal Palace in the southwestern district of the city was accidentally burned last night, it continued until 2:00 this morning. Its northern part was exacerbated by a sudden southerly wind. Fortunately, no one was injured. Hundreds of rare birds kept in the palace, which have always been famous in the world, were released during the fire and flew away. The Duke of Kent, on his fourth visit, attended a banquet somewhere last night. After the end of the banquet, he rushed to the scene after hearing the news, immediately changed into a leather cloak and long boots, and went in and out of dangerous areas with firefighters until 3:00 in the morning before returning. When the fire was at its fiercest, 56 water hoses were pouring water at the same time, so the two clock towers in the Crystal Palace were preserved. By dawn, only 10 water hoses continued to pour water. There were thousands of people surrounding and watching, all of whom stayed up all night. (Havas Electric, 1st)

(London) The famous Crystal Palace in this city was completely destroyed by fire tonight. The four walls of the palace were made of glass, which immediately collapsed and shattered into pieces, the sound of which could be heard several miles away. The Crystal Palace was first completed in Hyde Park in 1851, as part of the exhibition hall at the time. Afterwards, it was rebuilt as a public amusement place on Norwood Hill Street in the southwestern district of London. It is no longer as well-known as it used to be, but there are still many Londoners who visit it every day, especially children. Now that it has been destroyed by fire, London has lost a popular amusement park. (Havas Electric, 30th)

(London) The palace has been a famous place of entertainment in London for 85 years. Since it was completed in 1851, the grand events held there cannot be fully recorded. General Manager Sir Buckland said, "I am very saddened that there will never be a Crystal Palace again." The building was adequately insured against fire, but there are many treasures that cannot be obtained with money. The total loss is about £1.5 million. (Reuters, 1st)

French Chamber of Deputies Discusses Labor-Management Arbitration Bill 81

(Paris) The Chamber of Deputies recently began debating the compulsory arbitration bill for labor-management disputes today. The bill argues that all labor-management disputes should be submitted to the National Vocational Joint Committee for conciliation. Once conciliation fails, arbitrators should be separately elected by both parties to the dispute to make a ruling. If an agreement cannot be reached, the Prime Minister will appoint a super-arbitrator to make a decision. The candidates for this super-arbitrator should be jointly proposed by the General Confederation of Labor and the Employers' Federation, and selected by the Prime Minister. (Havas Electric, 1st)

Key Members of the Japanese Army and Navy Ministries Arrive in Tianjin Repeatedly to Convey the Intentions of the Central Leadership and Prepare for War Strategies; Japanese Destroyers Suddenly Arrive in Tanggu 83

Tianjin Correspondence: The Japanese Garrison Headquarters here has held repeated meetings to discuss the problem of bandits and puppets violating Suiyuan. Following the arrival of Lieutenant General Itagaki, Chief of Staff of the Japanese Kwantung Army, those who came to Tianjin for negotiations included Lieutenant General Sato, Military Councilor of the Japanese Army Ministry. He arrived on the 27th from Changchun, transiting, to meet with Field Marshal Tashiro, Commander of the Japanese Army, to convey the intentions of the Japanese central leadership. He met with Usukawa, head of the Japanese Residents' Association, Tamura, head of the Japanese Veterans Association, and others in Tianjin for consecutive days to exchange views on general important work during the so-called extraordinary period, and to investigate our movements. He plans to go to Peiping on December 5 to meet with Kawabe, commander of the Japanese Brigade, and Matsushita, the Japanese military attaché stationed in Peiping, and then transfer to Qingdao and Jinan on the 11th to meet with military attachés Tanizaki and Ishino in those two places. He will arrive in Shanghai on the 18th to meet with military attachés Kita and Kusumoto, and Commander Okawa of the Japanese Marines, and is scheduled to return home before the 25th to report. The Japanese military will base its preparations for strategies against us on the results of his activities. It is also reported that Ishihara Kanetsugu, head of the Operations Section of the Japanese General Staff, and Imada Shintaro, head of the Intelligence Section, arrived in Tianjin on the 28th of this month. These two brought plans from the Japanese General Staff for the event of war. According to their itinerary, they first went to Changchun from Tokyo at the beginning of this month to contact the Japanese Kwantung Army Headquarters, and also attended the meeting of the Japanese Kwantung Army Division Commanders stationed in Manchuria on November 20. After synthesizing the opinions of that meeting, they came to Tianjin. On the day of their arrival in Tianjin, Commander Tashiro of the Japanese Army convened a meeting at the Haiguang Temple Headquarters, attended by Hashimoto Gun, Chief of Staff of the Headquarters, and Staff Officers Iida, Wachi, Senda, and Ikeda, as well as Regiment Commanders Kayashima, Mutaguchi, and Suzuki. Ishihara reported the intentions of the Japanese General Staff and the opinions of the Japanese Kwantung Army Headquarters. Then Hashimoto Gun reported on the current situation of the troops stationed in North China and the deployment of the Japanese army. The meeting lasted from 2 PM to 6 PM. At 9:15 AM on the 29th, Ishihara and Imada left Tianjin to visit Kawabe and Matsushita in Beiping to exchange views. On the 30th, they flew to Zhangbei and Shangdu to conduct reconnaissance and meet with De Wang and Li Shouxin to discuss matters, then transferred to Changchun to confer with Ueda and Itagaki. They will return home at the beginning of next month. In the future, the war strategies instructed by the Japanese General Staff will also take the opinions of the Kwantung Army and the Tianjin Garrison Army as a certain point to carry out production. It is also heard that the two military headquarters have quite a bit of consultation on the planning of the Suiyuan affair. Ishihara's additional task is to reconcile the opinions of both parties to make them consistent, so that the steps will not be chaotic when launching the campaign. After the Japanese Kwantung Army Headquarters issued a statement on the Suiyuan incident on the 28th, the future war situation has been shown to the world. Although the Peiping-Tianjin area is not within the war zone, the situation is still very tense under the influence. From the 28th, the Japanese Second Infantry Regiment and part of the Artillery Regiment, combined with part of the Chemical Warfare Team, held temporary large-scale exercises in Dabi Village, Fan Zizhuang, and other places in the suburbs of Tianjin. More than 1,600 people from various arms of service participated, divided into attacking and defending parties with the goal of vying for Tianjin. The exercise time was from 8 AM to 10 PM, camping in the wild until December 2nd. At the same time, Commander Tashiro of the Japanese Army, accompanied by Chief of Staff Hashimoto and Staff Officers Senda and Asai, went to Tanggu and the east to Tangshan, Qinhuangdao, Luanxian, and Yu County on November 30 to inspect the troops. Also, on the evening of the 28th, the destroyer "Sasan" from Lushun Port sailed into Tanggu Port for berthing, preparing for the protection of overseas Chinese in case of unexpected events. Such actions seem to have the intention of threatening Hebei and Chahar. (30th)

A Record of Inspecting Suiyuan: Our Troops in Eastern Suiyuan and Suihua Have Very Solid Defense Lines; Extremely Many Military Supplies Were Obtained When Capturing Bailingmiao 84

Beiping Correspondence: Since the puppet bandit troops of Chahar and Bei repeatedly invaded Eastern and Northern Suiyuan, in order to understand the truth of the front, the reporter left Peiping on the 24th of last month to conduct an on-the-spot investigation along the Peiping-Suiyuan line. During that time, I passed through Datong, Fengzhen, Jining (Pingdiquan), Honggeertu, Suiyuan, Baotou, Bailingmiao and other places, and separately visited military and political figures in various places. After a week, I returned to Peiping yesterday. The report on the findings of this trip is as follows:

The Actual Strength of the Puppet Bandits

After the reporter set off, he separately inquired about the strength of the puppet bandits. It is learned that after De Wang expanded the Mongolian army and occupied the six counties of Chahar North, Wang Ying's bandit troops followed and went there. Finally, Li Shouxin's puppet army also arrived from Dolon. After the puppet bandits gathered in northern Chahar, Li Shouxin's puppet army, De Wang's Mongol puppet army, and Wang Ying's bandit army stood divided. Li's troops were organized into the First Army, under the jurisdiction of Yin Baoshan and other troops, claiming to be four divisions, totaling 10,000 people, stationed in Shangdu, Huade, Nanhaogou, Daqinggou (that is, Shangyi), Yin's troops stationed in Shangdu, and Li sometimes traveled between Nanhaogou and Daqinggou. De Wang's Mongol army, under the puppet military Bao Yueqing, Zhuoshihai, Mu Zhenbao and other Mongolian security teams, numbered no more than 10,000 people, mostly in Jiabus, Bailingmiao, and other places. De Wang himself often went to Jiabus and occasionally flew to Bailingmiao to direct everything. Wang Ying led Zhang Wanxin's First Division, Jin Jiasan and Ma Yutian's Brigade, and the seven or eight thousand people of the pistol regiment and the guard regiment, stationed in the Tonglingdi area, also claiming to be four divisions. The three divisions occupy the line from Bailingmiao, via Tumuerte, Honggentu, Dayanhai, and northern Xinghe, to Nanhaogou, Zhangbei, and Chongli.

Strengthening Jining's Defenses

After the puppet army completed its layout in Chahar, Shangyi was thousands of miles away from Xinghe, and Shangdu was only a hundred miles away from Jining. Jining is an important town on the Peiping-Suiyuan Railway and a pivotal point between Shanxi and Suiyuan Provinces. For months, they have been trying to achieve their goals at any time. In order to ensure Suiyuan's transportation, our officers and soldiers, aware of their responsibility to defend the territory, have been extra careful in their defenses, making it extremely difficult for the puppet bandits to succeed.

Failed Invasions

At the beginning of last month, the bandits, believing that the time had come, once invaded Xinghe but were repelled by Gao Tuan of the Li Division of the defending army. In the middle of the month, the bandit puppet army concentrated more than 1,000 infantry, cavalry, and artillery to invade Honggeertu (that is, Honggentu) west of Shangdu and north of Taolin. Zhao Chengshou's cavalry, Fu Zuoyi and Li Fuying's infantry, and other troops separately fought back fiercely for three days and nights. The bandit puppet army even used airplanes to help in the battle. On the third day, three aircraft were finally shot down by our army's accurate artillery team. At this point, the entire puppet bandit force retreated. When the aircraft were injured and descended, the local military and civilians cheered the situation. General Fu Zuoyi specially awarded 1,000 yuan to show encouragement. It is reported that the bandits' invasion plan was to invade Wulanhua from Honggeertu in the west, go straight to Baotou via Guyang, and at the same time another group was planned to cross hundreds of miles of uninhabited area from Shangdu to Jiutai, Shitai, and Shiyitai, directly reaching Wuchuan and taking Guihua. Another team would feint an attack on Xinghe from Nanhaogou to try to contain the national army's strength. Although the soldiers of our national army ate fried rice in the freezing weather every day, their spirits were lifted, and their morale was high. They did not feel bitter at all when fighting with the bandits and puppets.

Chuan-Shi's Calm

General Fu Zuoyi, as the chairman of Suiyuan Province and commander of the 35th Army, personally presided over everything. Since the suppression of bandits and armies, he has been calm and relaxed. Dressed in an admiral's uniform, he did not take it off all day, and was busy deploying military affairs on one hand and diligently entertaining on the other, and his attitude was as if he was not tired at all. He did not sleep for two days while planning the attack on Bailingmiao, so his face was slightly thinner. In Suiyuan, the people felt a little panicked before the military was launched. After the bandits were disturbed and defeated, the people felt more stable. The local area was as usual, without any war state, and life was also very stable. However, the inspection of passengers was very strict. There were military police inspections in the trains from Datong to Suiyuan, and the passengers' surnames and origins were inquired in detail to prevent spies from taking the opportunity to mix in.

Zhao Chengshou's Talk

When the reporter passed through Jining, he visited Zhao Chengshou, the commander of the cavalry army. According to him, his headquarters has been stationed on the border of Shanxi and Suiyuan for several years, and the bandits have been suppressed. However, there are now puppet bandits invading again, and the officers and soldiers are extremely indignant. On the 13th of this month, I went to Pingdiquan with Chairman Fu from Sui to learn that the puppet bandits in northern Chahar had the potential to strike a blow. At that time, the foremost Qian of our army was Honggeertu, and the garrison there was only two companies. When the telegraph order was sent to the regiment commander to order the troops to defend to the death, and to send teams to reinforce within twelve hours. On the 16th, the bandits attacked with 3,000 infantry, cavalry, and artillery, intending to capture Pingdiquan and cut off our traffic. So the fierce battle began and continued until dawn on the 18th. The bandits even invaded our main positions with four bandit aircraft to help in the battle. Our artillery team shot down three of the aircraft and completely defeated the bandits. At the same time, because the puppet bandits occupied Bailingmiao, Suiyuan and Northern Suiyuan were threatened at times. On the 23rd, my cavalry division, Chairman Fu's infantry, and Commander Wang's replenishment regiment were concentrated to launch a large-scale attack at 9 PM that night. By 9 AM the next morning, the temple was completely recovered. The military supplies, food, and other items that the bandits had stockpiled in the temple for many years were all obtained by our army. This is the result of the soldiers' dedication and clear understanding of justice. In the future, we must continue to work hard to strengthen the country for the country.

Wang Jingguo's Talk

After the reporter arrived in Suiyuan, Wang Jingguo also arrived in Guihua, and immediately sent a name card to visit. Briefly noted the following conversation: "After I was ordered to take over the 19th Army, because the military headquarters was located in Taiyuan, most of the 70th Division was stationed in Suiyuan, so I have been traveling between Shanxi and Suiyuan for years. I have entrusted Brigade Commander Tian Shumei to be responsible for the defenses of western Suiyuan. I heard in the military that the Bailingmiao puppet bandits were preparing to attack us, so I immediately set off and returned. Before the Suiyuan were captured, I heard that Bailingmiao had been recovered, and I was very happy. Because I have matters to be discussed with Chairman Fu, I came to Sui first, and I will go to western Suiyuan to handle military affairs and inspect the reclamation area within days. The reclamation situation this year is still good, and I will plan the reclamation work for next year when I go this time," he said.

Li Fuying's Talk

On his way back, the reporter got off at Datong and visited Commander Li Fuying, who gave the following speech, "In this battle, in which the bandits and puppets invaded westward, our army, under the principle of defending the soil and resisting insults, is determined to "have bandits without me, and have me without bandits" and is determined to fight to the end. Although my department has been defeated by the command of Director Yan and Commander Fu, and the bandits and puppets attacking Xinghe have been defeated. Even though part of my army participated in the Battle of Honggeertu, it is the duty of soldiers to serve in the borderlands. However, I am extremely ashamed to have been visited by people from all walks of life and to have received the enthusiastic condolences of the elders of the whole country. According to reports, the bandits and puppets are now gathering troops and planning a large-scale invasion to the west, which shows that the border trouble is in full swing, and the small victories in the past battles are not enough to talk about. From now on, we can only encourage the soldiers to be more vigilant, in order to strengthen the border defense, to comfort the people of the country, and to fulfill the duties of the army. I also hope that people across the country will supervise and guide us at any time," he said (to be continued)

The Bandits and Puppets Are Preparing Their Main Forces, Attempting to Counterattack Bailingmiao; Officers from a Certain Party Are Arriving in Jiabus Temple from Dolon; The Remnants of the Bandits and Puppets Are Gradually Gathering Towards Pangjiang and Shangdu 85

Shangdu Correspondence: Since Bailingmiao was recovered by our Suiyuan army, it has directly dealt a huge blow to the bandits and puppets, and indirectly created a huge obstacle to a certain party's policy of opening up Chahar and Suiyuan. Now the leaders of a certain party and the bandits and puppets are holding secret meetings at Jiabus Temple (that is, the Huade Administrative Bureau), with very strict security. According to the bandits and puppets, they will never easily give up Bailingmiao. It is not only important in terms of combat strategy, but also the loss of military supplies is indeed not subsidized. Therefore, they are actively preparing their main forces in an attempt to counterattack. Under this situation, the bandits and puppets are also very active. Their situation is described below:

More Than 100 Officers From a Certain Party Arrive at the Temple

On November 26, more than 100 officers from a certain party traveled in five cars from Dolon to Jiabus Temple, arriving on the 27th. They brought many military Chahar-Suiyuan maps and various forms. In addition, a large amount of military supplies and coal were continuously transported from Zhangbei to Jiabus Temple and Shangdu. According to internal sources of the bandits and puppets, more than 3,000 new-style guns were lost in the two failures of Bailingmiao and Honggeertu, some of which were taken by the Suiyuan army, and some were taken by defecting troops and deserters. On the 26th, ten heavy trucks of new guns were transported from Zhangbei and distributed to various departments for replenishment. As for cotton-padded uniforms, six trucks have now been transported to Shangdu.

It Is Difficult to Build Fortifications in the Cold Weather

Since the national army recaptured Bailingmiao, the bandit puppet Mongols who attacked northern Suiyuan fled to the hinterland of northern Suiyuan and Pangjiang Erlian and other places. Most of them retreated east to Shangdu. Now, the bandits and puppets who have fled to Pangjiang and the hinterland are gathering towards Pangjiang, reaching more than 7,000 people, and will also be opening towards Shangdu. On the 27th, more than 1,000 artillery soldiers from the Jia Ge Ying area opened to Rehe. Except for the Gan Ying and Li Shouxin armies stationed in Shangdu, there are also 2,000 Rehe puppet soldiers under Wang Jingxiu, who have opened to the west to join Li Zhenming's puppet troops in guarding the Qianqian. The attitudes of the chief rebels are still determined to be reckless, and they are forcing laborers to rush to build defensive projects day and night. However, due to the cold weather, progress is difficult and it is not easy to complete quickly. The bandits and puppets are urging the construction. As for all the wounded soldiers, no one cares about them, and the rescue equipment is also very inadequate. Many people die one after another due to the cold weather and excessive blood loss.

Wang Ying's Bandits Have Different Ambitions

Wang Ying's bandit troops have been increasingly despised by a certain party since their defeat in Hongzhen. Their subordinates also have different ambitions. On the night of November 26, Wang and Yin Baoshan held a secret meeting, and they almost broke down on the spot due to disagreements. Other middle and lower-level officers have also been secretly discussing in recent days. A certain party is even more suspicious of them. Li Shouxin's army has now been sent to monitor Wang's actions. As for Wang's subordinates, there are still more than 3,000 people. Wang has sent more than 60 of his confidants to secretly recruit troops in the interior from Shangdu on the 28th.

Bandits and Puppet Intelligence Is Sent to Changchun Daily

The activities of the bandits and puppets in northern Chahar are reported to Changchun via radio every day. All radio transmitting and receiving technical personnel are nationals of a certain country, and there are also troops from a certain country guarding them. In Guyuan, Dolon, and places adjacent to Rehe, bandit troops from the Hot Border are constantly arriving, and residents are extremely panicked. Therefore, the current situation in northern Chahar is already in an extremely terrifying state. Those with a little property have fled to various places in the inland one after another. (28th)

Suzhou Memorial Service for Martyr Zhou Mingyang 86

Zhou Mingyang, a student of Cuiying Middle School, participated in a propaganda team and set off for propaganda on the Six-Three Anti-Smoking Memorial Day this year. He unfortunately fell into the river and died on the way. The teachers and students of the school have held a memorial service. For the sake of commemorating Zhou Mingyang, the Anti-Smoking Committee here has initiated the establishment of a memorial tablet at the foot of Tiger Hill to commemorate it, and specially elected Zhang Yanpeng to plan and proceed, and also recommended Wu Zengshan to draft the memorial tablet inscription.

Nantong Two Robber Bandits Executed by Firing Squad 87

Xie Sheng Cotton House in Sanyu Town used a car from the city to transport 15,000 yuan back to the town, but it was robbed by bandits in Jiujiaba. The bandits were captured by the detective team and handed over to the Fourth District Security Command for interrogation. On the 30th, the two chief culprits, Ji Youen and Cao Yingde, were approved by the provincial government to be sentenced to death and were taken to the scene of the incident and executed by firing squad. The accomplices Ji Rongfang was sentenced to twelve years in prison, and Cao Changyuan and Cao Yangshi were sentenced to seven years in prison each, and sent to the Fourth Jiangsu Prison for execution.

Relief for Coastal Fishermen 88

The fishermen in the nine fishing areas along the coast of Tongzhou Prefecture are having a difficult time making a living. The Fishermen's Association has requested relief from the provincial and ministerial departments. The special commissioner's office and the financial community are discussing the provision of fishery loans and the organization of a fish product transportation and marketing cooperative, which is in progress.

Taicang Prisoners Go on Hunger Strike to Support Suiyuan 89

The prisoners Xue Wu et al. of Taicang County Prison, Guardhouse, and the separate confinement area for drug offenders, in the name of pseudo-bandits invading Suiyuan, and our front-line soldiers, are defending the country and killing enemies in the freezing cold, with great differences in hardship and happiness. The prisoners, although deprived of freedom, still have obligations. Therefore, on the 29th, they voluntarily went on a one-day hunger strike, and the remaining food expenses of forty yuan and two cents were submitted to the front by Warden Zhang via the county government. In addition, the town and rural merchants, organizations, and groups in the county held a one-day sports event, and the remaining support for Suiyuan was also very enthusiastic.

Wuxi A Wall of Brothers Leads to a Homicide 90

Gu Arong, a resident of Dai Lane, Nanfangquan, District 3, over forty years old, was a farmer. At 9 AM the day before yesterday, he brought self-brewed white wine to his biological mother, Gu Yangshi, at Gedaiqiao, and drank with his younger brother, Gu Apei. Unexpectedly, Yangshi was seriously ill at the time. At that time, the two brothers discussed how to handle the funeral after their mother's death and how to distribute the economy. They disagreed and immediately took action. As a result, Arong was injured and died. Xiao Ruyuan, the head of the 84th map, and Gu Haiwu, the head of the 14th Bao, reported to the local court and requested an autopsy. Yesterday (1st), at 9 AM, Prosecutor Shen led officials to the countryside for an autopsy.

Yichang Warehouse Was Careless 91

Yichang Warehouse in Xixing Town outside the West Gate of the county, formerly the site of Nansui Sheng Warehouse, has always been used to stockpile rice. The owner of the warehouse is Hua Yizhi, a gentry in the county, and the manager is Hua Junmin. There are more than 200 warehouses in total, and the business is developed. At 4 PM on the 30th of last month, a fire suddenly broke out in the kitchen in the southwest corner of the warehouse, spreading to the nearby firewood room and warehouse, and it was out of control, piercing through the roof. The fire brigades and police stations in each section immediately drove the dragons to the scene to draw water for rescue. It took about an hour before it was extinguished. A total of eight warehouses were burned down, and the loss was quite large. At the same time, Qian Yingsheng, Wu Asan, and other three families in Houchun Village, Xicao Lane, Zhouxin Town, District 3, also suffered from carelessness, with a loss of more than a thousand yuan. Also, the home of Wu Jinchun on Yantou Street, Xuedian Town, District 8, suddenly reported a fire, which spread to the neighbors and turned into scorched earth. The situation was terrible.

Joint Defense by Land and Water in Eight Counties 92

The Security Command of the Second District Administrative Inspectorate of Jiangsu Province believes that at this time of national crisis, local security should be effectively maintained in order to pacify the people. Seven measures for joint defense by land and water have been stipulated: 1. Joint defense by land and water shall be implemented within this district. 2. Eliminate scattered bandits, hold regular meetings and patrols. 3. Use the Baojia organization to investigate and arrest bandits. 4. Register evil people. 5. Install river fences on small rivers. 6. The Baojia chiefs of each township shall persuade the people that if a robbery occurs, they shall promptly report to the nearest land and water defense area for pursuit. 7. The land and water public security organs shall pay attention to the junction of the province and county and jointly prevent it. Yesterday, Commissioner Zang ordered the land and water public security organs of Wuxi, Wujin, Wuxian, Wujiang, Jiangyin, Changshu, Kunshan, and Taicang to comply with them.

Popular News: Jiaotong Bank Theft Case Solved 93

Following the major theft at the Jiaotong Bank in this city, the Public Security Bureau's detective team arrested and detained Yan Genfu, the bank's cook, who was heavily suspected. Subsequent investigation revealed that Ding Guifang, the foreman of the construction site next to the bank, was also involved. Stolen goods were found in the dormitory of an employee named Gui Shensheng, and a large amount of stolen goods was also found in the home of a relative of an employee. It was determined that this case was premeditated and organized. The relevant employees have been arrested and detained in the Public Security Bureau. The truth of the case has been fully clarified, but the exact amount involved will be determined after the bank manager returns from Qingdao and conducts an audit.

Jinhua: Legal Entities Request Re-measurement of Land 95

The land registration and survey in Jinhua County is riddled with errors, leading to repeated disputes. Representatives from the county's farmers' association Cao Jingtai, education association Wang Zhensheng, chamber of commerce Cheng Shirong, labor union Huang Xiuchan, and citizens Fang Hao, Qian Xietong, Liao Yingduo, Qian Youren, Tang Bingkun, and others, jointly submitted a document to the Zhejiang Provincial Government requesting a re-measurement of land in order to clarify property rights and alleviate the people's suffering. An excerpt of the original submission is as follows:

"The land under the county's jurisdiction has always been based on contracts. Except for communal properties, which are referred to as a certain hall or room, all grain households are registered in their own names. The grain registers clearly record the number, acreage, location, and category of each plot, with very few errors. However, the previous county magistrate, Chen Kaisi, under the guise of implementing new policies, hastily initiated a land registration and survey. Last July, he recruited over a hundred students, calling them a rural work personnel training class, and hired three or four college students as trainers. After more than a month of training, they were dispatched to various locations to carry out the work. From the very beginning, the process was so sloppy. As for the survey itself, neither the landowners nor the tenants were notified. In each village, a random shepherd boy was hired as a guide, leading to absurd mistakes. The surveyors did not measure the land or verify information, relying solely on oral records, perpetuating errors. As a result, local names and plot locations became garbled, and the distinction between public and private ownership was blurred. Even irrigation systems were arbitrarily registered without any supporting evidence, which will inevitably lead to major disputes in times of drought. In summary, the problems are as follows: (1) Disruption of the irrigation system; (2) Arbitrary division of land into upper, middle, and lower grades, with corresponding variations in acreage; (3) Omissions in registration; (4) Incorrect or duplicate registration; (5) Fraudulent claims; (6) Re-measurement fees: This survey is riddled with errors, and the people have collectively requested corrections. A so-called re-measurement is being conducted, but in reality, no actual measurement is taking place. Yet, a fee of $1.20 is charged for each re-measured parcel; (7) Unilateral applications: Re-measurement is granted based on the application of one party without notifying the other party involved; (8) Increased acreage: Surveyors often record the acreage of mountain fields as being ten or even dozens of times greater than the original acreage. When asked why the discrepancy, they claim it is based on visual estimation. The surveyors can manipulate the acreage at will, and their salaries are based on the acreage measured, so listing more acres means more income; (9) Excessive collection of land ownership certificate fees: The county government claims that the survey is complete, but less than 30-40% of the registrations have been verified. Yet, the people are being ordered to exchange their land ownership certificates. The certificates are nowhere to be seen, but the price of the certificate has already risen to seven cents each. The above are just the most glaring examples. Other issues, such as surveyors abusing their power for personal gain and oppressing the local population, are minor matters. The representatives previously appealed to the former county magistrate, who was responsible for handling the matter, but were forced to wait for its completion. The problems have only increased with time, and the consequences are unimaginable. We can no longer remain silent. The land ownership certificates have not yet been issued, and it is not too late to rectify the situation. Therefore, we dare to present the circumstances and the resulting problems, pleading for a thorough investigation and the complete overturning of this flawed policy, with a re-measurement of land to alleviate the people's suffering and attach importance to land administration."

After Completing Attendance at the Pacific Society Meeting, Hu Shi Returns to China and Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday; Public Lecture at the YMCA at 7:30 PM Tonight 113

The Central News Agency reporter recorded the following details:

Friends Welcomed: The ship docked at the Gonghexiang Pier. Those who went to welcome him included Li Dachao, section chief of the Municipal Government; Zhou Jue, director of the Shanghai office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs; Cheng Haifeng, head of the China branch of the National Labor Bureau; Zhu Changnian, superintendent of the Jianghai Customs; Xu Xinliu, of the Banking Association; Yan Fuqing, of the Chinese Red Cross Society; Yao Xi, of the Aviation Association; Liu Yuwan, of the China branch of the Pacific Society; Li Zhaohuan, president of Jiaotong University; Jian Youwen, member of the Legislative Yuan; and Xue Dubi, and others, totaling dozens of people. Mr. Hu's demeanor was the same as before, and he was slightly more obese than when he went abroad. After exchanging greetings with the welcoming personnel, he went directly to the International Hotel to rest.

Hernia Fully Recovered: Mr. Hu met with reporters on the ship and gave a speech, saying that the representatives who had returned to China earlier had already reported on the proceedings of attending the Pacific Society meeting. He will give a more detailed report at the YMCA tomorrow night (tonight). While in the United States, he suffered from a hernia (Veutal Hornia), which was surgically repaired. He had an appendicitis attack four years ago, which was surgically removed. This time, a part of the intestine protruded into the gap in the skin that had already been operated on, causing the condition. After being sewn up, he has recovered, and is using a truss to support the affected area. Reports that he had appendicitis are not true.

Recent Situation in the United States: I was in the United States for four months and left on November 12th. In the next four years, the people of that country will definitely support the government more, and the government's power will definitely be strengthened.

Good Feelings Toward China: Regarding the attitude of the United States towards China, American newspapers previously had some misunderstandings about Chinese public opinion. Recently, because our country has been completely unified and its diplomacy has been quite tough, based on the principle of not losing sovereignty, the public opinion has been unanimously praised. The president of the Associated Press, He Huaide, after returning to the United States from China, wrote an essay praising all the construction of our country and said that China has undoubtedly become a unified country.

Returning to Beijing Tomorrow Night: Regarding the Japan-Germany agreement and the recent situation in the Far East, Mr. Hu said that he had been out of touch with the situation for many days during his travels. He also said that he only represented Peking University, Nankai University, and the Academia Sinica to attend the Pacific Society meeting. While in the United States, Harvard University and the University of Puget Sound awarded him honorary doctorate degrees. He is scheduled to return to Beijing on the evening of the 3rd.

Supervisory and Assessment Methods in the Movement to Implement Free Education 114

In addition to classes and lectures, this year's training class for free education personnel from the Ministry of Education also discussed practical issues related to free education. The National Free Education Committee of the Ministry of Education also submitted issues for discussion. The discussions focused on issues related to supervision and assessment of free education. All decided opinions and methods will generally be followed by the Ministry of Education and various provinces and cities in the future. The general methods of supervision and assessment are summarized below, which should be welcomed by national supervisors and those administering free education.

Regarding Supervision:

A. Measures for dividing free education supervision areas between the central and local governments. After discussion, it was decided that this area-based supervision should first be implemented at the level of the Ministry, provinces, and cities. Counties and elementary school districts do not need to be divided. The division of areas in each province and city should be based on teacher training areas or administrative inspectorate areas, with room for flexibility. Ministry supervision personnel should supervise the free education areas under their jurisdiction at least once a year. Provincial and municipal supervision personnel should supervise the free education areas under their jurisdiction at least once per semester. Supervision personnel from the Ministry and provinces should focus on random inspections, while municipal supervision personnel should focus on comprehensive supervision. For comprehensive inspections, Ministry supervisors should selectively inspect at least one-fifth of the counties and cities under their jurisdiction each year, and provincial supervisors should selectively inspect at least one-third of the elementary school districts under their jurisdiction each year. The duties of supervisors at all levels should be stipulated by the Ministry of Education, and the Ministry of Education or the National Free Education Committee should formulate standards for comprehensive and detailed inspections of free education. The number of free education inspectors should be determined by each province and city based on actual needs. B. The titles of free education inspectors should be standardized. After discussion, it was decided that the titles should be uniformly designated as "Supervisors," and the Ministry should issue a circular to all provinces and cities for compliance. C. How should the administrative structures of educational supervision be communicated and connected? After discussion, it was decided that in addition to ordinary administrative liaison, supervision meetings should be held every year (the Ministry of Education convenes meetings of provincial supervisors, the Education Department convenes meetings of district supervisors, the administrative district convenes meetings of county supervisors, and the county education administrative organs convene meetings of supervision personnel from each school district). Administrative organizations at all levels should improve their organization with reference to the supervisory outlines of Anhui Province and the guidance conference methods of Zhejiang Province. If there are more than three supervision personnel at each level, a director may be appointed to coordinate their efforts and facilitate communication. Supervisors at all levels must first review the reports on supervision within their districts by the higher-level supervisors before conducting their supervision. Lower-level supervisors should accept the guidance of higher-level supervisors. The supervision personnel of the education administrative organs should liaise effectively with the guidance personnel of the education organs (as already implemented in Jiangsu). Supervision personnel should primarily conduct supervision by district, as this facilitates communication between higher and lower levels. D. How should the duties of supervisors at all levels (originally "督學," changed to "視導人員") be defined with regard to the work of supervising free education? After discussion, it was decided that a clear statement should be included in the regulations for supervisors at all levels, specifying the supervision of compulsory education, as well as defining supervisory principles, supervisory focus, supervisory points, supervisory methods, supervisory steps, and supervisory reports. In addition, standards for supervising free education should be established based on the regulations for supervisors at all levels. E. It was decided that supervision of free education should pay special attention to nineteen items, including school equipment, administrative structure, student enrollment, assessment, and district division. F. It was decided that supervision personnel should provide guidance and encourage teachers to improve and conduct research on their own initiative. G. Regarding the continuing education and research methods for supervision personnel, after discussion, it was decided that they should browse newly published education books and newspapers, organize reading groups and visit groups, hold meetings of supervision personnel, conduct lectures and training for supervision personnel, conduct correspondence research, and the Ministry of Education should compile and distribute a catalogue of books and newspapers that supervision personnel should read to all provinces and cities for reference.

Regarding Assessment:

In addition to stipulating various assessment items, methods of calculation, and requesting the Ministry of Education to consult with each province and city to formulate various reward and punishment measures based on the effective methods of implementing free education in each province and city, regarding the reward measures for local people who voluntarily run free education, it was decided to request the Ministry of Education to formulate reward measures, paying attention to both spiritual and material rewards. For spiritual rewards, written or certificate formats should be used. For material rewards, a portion of the funds from the free education budget or other surplus education funds should be used to subsidize the schools as a reward to local people who voluntarily run excellent elementary schools. The advantages and disadvantages of mutual supervision between supervision personnel and education organs were also discussed. It was generally agreed that the exchange supervision in Jiangsu Province and Shanghai City was quite effective, and other provinces and cities could refer to it. The advantages are that it can prevent supervision personnel from acting on emotions, using public office for private gain, and prevent unfair facts from occurring. Supervision reports can be accurate because both parties are supervising each other and dare not make false reports. If the supervised personnel are treated unfairly, they can have the opportunity to defend themselves. The disadvantages are that as a result of mutual supervision, they can attack each other, each sticking to their own version, and the truth is not easy to clarify. As a result of mutual supervision, the responsible superior shows distrust of the supervision personnel he has appointed. If the directly appointed person cannot be trusted, then the indirectly supervised personnel are even less trustworthy. If the two parties collude and cooperate in intelligence, it will be more difficult for the responsible superior to investigate. Finally, the conference decided that the nature of education supervision is different from that of ordinary administrative official inspections, and attention should be paid to active guidance. There is no need for mutual supervision, because mutual supervision makes it impossible for the education sector to trust each other from top to bottom, which easily leads to adverse results.

Food: Everyone is Storing Grass and Grain; Flour Price Has Reached Four Yuan, Unprecedented Since the Establishment of the Exchange; The Market Was Stalled Due to the One-Corner Limit 117

Yesterday's flour market, after the opening in the morning, the market in each month showed a crazy rise again. The price of foreign wheat was quoted in Chicago, up another corner, Canada up three or four corners, and Liverpool up one penny. As the world wheat price has been rising, and the domestic wheat has been falling again, and the prices of all kinds of goods have been rising without falling, the background is as if the whole world is shrouded in the clouds of war, causing people to panic. Storing grass and grain is so urgent that there is no time to choose, and everyone is preparing with raw materials. The price increases in the market are all based on this. When the price opened, this month immediately rose by eight points, and then continued to rise by two points, while in one transaction it fell back by two or three points. January started, and it rose by seven or eight points at first, but in April it rose by one corner compared to the previous month. Therefore, after the second transaction, except for this month, which was still two and a half cents short, the rest all rose to one corner. The turnover reached 700,000 to 800,000 in half a day. When the market opened in the afternoon, the exchange temporarily increased the margin to 500 yuan, and the market sentiment in each month was less traded due to the one-corner limit, so it was virtually stalled. Observing this kind of market price is the highest record since the establishment of the exchange, and the surrounding environment is still impossible to remedy, so the future storm is really beyond the ordinary speculation.

Foreign Wheat Continues to Rise; Domestic Wheat Rises Unprecedentedly; April Futures Have Reached Six Yuan and Ninety-Two Cents 118

Yesterday's wheat market, after the opening in the morning, the rise of the market in each month was as intense as if it had reached boiling point, because the price of foreign wheat has continued to rise consistently since the end of the previous month and yesterday's report, especially Liverpool. This situation is no different from the world's unanimous military preparations, and not only wheat has continued to rise, but also the prices of various domestic oils have also followed step by step. Therefore, after the opening, people's hearts were greatly stirred. The opening price in this month immediately rose by one corner and three or four points, and from January onwards, it also followed the rise by one corner and two or three points to one corner and eight points. When the market opened in the afternoon, the market price rose to the limit price due to the sharp rise in the flour market, so the buying interest was even stronger. Except for the old longs who sold back, there were very few new shorts. Therefore, each month continued to rise by five, six or seven points. For example, the rise in April reached two and a half corners. The highest point in the market reached six yuan and ninety-two cents. The rise was unprecedented, and the price was also a landmark. The current wheat market is hoarding, and very few transactions are seen. The ordinary high price opened at six yuan and two corners, followed by zero and nine points, with a transaction volume of over a thousand bags.

Under the Control of Dalian, Soybean Cake Prices are Rising Frequently; Countries are Storing Grain, Causing a Sharp Rise in the Dalian Market; This Port is Affected 119

Yesterday's standard market price of soybean cake was consistently rising, because the international war clouds are getting thicker, and there are rumors that various countries are storing grain, and the Dalian telegrams are also rising one after another. Yesterday, the price of soybeans rose by a corner, the price of oil rose by half a yuan, and the price of cake rose by four points. Therefore, the market sentiment was agitated, and the price of cotton yarn also rose sharply, which made the buyers even more excited. Various firms dared not sell out, so the opening price in the morning immediately soared. Although it was once suppressed by the liquidation of old longs, the new hoarding interest was very strong, and the result was still rising. The closing price of standard oil rose by four corners and a half to seven corners and a half, the standard soybeans rose by one corner and seven points and two or three points, and the standard cake also rose by three, five or six points.

Yesterday's soybean market, because the rising wind in Dalian was still strong, the standard soybeans opened on the exchange in this city, and the price soared by one or two corners, which caused the spot price of soybean oil to continue to rise by two corners, and the price of soybean cake continued to rise by a few points. Therefore, the soybean price rose again by four or five points, but the oil mills, seeing that the price continued to rise, inevitably reduced their appetite for hoarding. Therefore, the rise in yesterday's market was slight. Yesterday, a total of seven carts of beans from Siping Street, 3,000 bags of Za beans from Hankou, and 1,500 bags of Anqing beans were traded. The remaining beans were handled by this street for 700 to 800 bags.

Miscellaneous Grains are Rising; Only Ke Xian Rice is Relatively Flat and Soft 120

Ke Xian rice has been arriving in a steady stream recently. The daily arrivals have been as many as 10,000 bags or more, especially the arrivals from Hankou, Shashi, Hunan, and Jiangxi. Yesterday, all goods rose unanimously, and flour and wheat also saw a sharp rise of one corner and two corners. The rice price should have followed, but the arrivals were strong, and the Cantonese sales stopped, so the market was flat and soft. A total of 2,700 bags of Jiangxi rice, 127 bags of Xiang rice, and 753 bags of Yongwen rice were traded throughout the day, all of which were distributed by this street and Shantou. The market conditions were mostly similar to the previous market, but some were softer due to the suspension of Cantonese sales.

Why is So Much Grain Transported North? About 60,000 Bags in Just Three Days 121

In the past two days, the number of rice, flour, and miscellaneous grains transported from this city to North China has been considerable. The amount of flour is over one million bags, and the amount of rice is also over 150,000. Recently, it was heard that the market price in Tianjin and Yantai was slightly tired, but the exports from this city are still strong. Yesterday, the Yuping ship went to Tianjin, fully loaded with more than 25,000 bags of white rice. The Dingsheng ship, which exported this morning, also loaded more than 20,000 bags to Tianjin. A certain British ship, which will be exported tomorrow, also has 8,000 to 9,000 bags, which are being loaded today. In previous years, except for Ke Xian rice, very little Su Geng rice was transported to the north. However, in the past year, the transportation has been continuous. What is the purpose of this? It has not been revealed until now.

Bo Dao Sales Rely Solely on the North; Tianjin Merchants are the Main Force; The Purchases are all High-Quality Products 122

(South Shanghai) Yesterday, the sources of various merchants were slightly less than before, with a total of over eighty merchants, a total of 16,700 to 16,800 stones. Bo Dao still accounted for the majority. Fortunately, the purchasing power was still not weak. Merchants from Tianjin, Yantai, and Qingdao purchased over 6,000 bags of Bo Dao and 400 to 500 bags of Hou Geng. Retail sales still felt flat, so the market conditions did not fail to be stable. However, this time the purchasing power was dominated by Tianjin merchants, so they selected high-quality products for Bo Dao. As for the middle-grade goods, they were hesitant. As a result, the market conditions were that the high-quality goods were firm with a tight tone, the middle-grade market was flat with a soft undertone, the Hou Geng had little progress, the Du Jian still had a tired look, the Yang Jian goods were scarce and stable, and the Yin Yuan was also flat and correct. To predict the future trend, it still depends on the smoothness of purchasing power and the amount of source arrival.

(North Shanghai) Yesterday, the sources of various merchants in Hexia were forty-three merchants. The market merchants with quick selection made some purchases. The price of white Geng in the early market was soft by three or four points, and the evening market was firm. The arrival of Bo Dao was limited. Merchants from Tianjin, Yantai, and Dalian continued to purchase. The appetite of this street was still acceptable, and the price was firm. The price of Yang Jian was firm by two or three points, the price of Bu Gan Jian was firm, and the Yin Bian Yuan was peaceful. The rest of the rice was similar to before.

Yarn: Eight Yuan Achieved in One Go; Futures Yarn Suspended; --The Reason is-- Decline of Five Years, Things Must Return; Shortened Period, More Crazy Speculation 123

Until the Later Market, Both Sides were Deadlocked and Had Not Yet Opened

The yarn market rose wildly, with unstoppable momentum. The reason is that there is a strange shortage of spot yarn, and the buyer's appetite is quite strong. Therefore, the buying wind was set off, and new speculators rushed in, buying fiercely, with a strong absorption. The general floating air, seeing the bad environment, cut off without limiting the price, bearing the pain. Therefore, the market price soared, and the prices of each month were consistently suspended due to the rise. In the afternoon, they were still deadlocked and could not open a transaction. This kind of scene has never been seen since the exchange opened.

Unstoppable Buying Wind

The opening of the standard yarn in the previous market, each month rose sharply consistently. The reason is that the spot yarn sales market is still lively, and the factory's spot goods are out of stock. Therefore, the shorts were panicked, and the buyers came like a tide. The market opened step by step and jumped. The three transactions showed a slight setback. On the closing platform, only buying was heard, and very little selling. Each month jumped again, reaching the level of suspension. This kind of violent situation has been rare in the past five years. People's hearts are panic-stricken to the extreme. Checking the reasons, half is because the yarn market has been declining, so it has been five years. Things must return, the law of nature. Second, recently speculators have concentrated on the yarn and cotton market. The standard yarn period has been shortened, with only four months remaining. Once there is good news, the rising momentum is even more difficult to curb. As a result, each month rose by eight yuan to eight and a half yuan compared to the previous day's closing price. The afternoon was extended to 3:30 pm to open, and the long and short sides held different opinions. As a result, all of them could not open. However, the market situation was still chaotic. It is said that there are still some people doing things on the buying side. It was found that Jifeng sold 1,000 packages, Tongfu 2,250 packages, Hengyi 3,450 packages, Juxing 2,850 packages, Yiji 2,400 packages, Yuanda 1,150 packages, Gengfeng 2,600 packages, Ruida 2,150 packages, Shenji 4,100 packages, Taichang 1,550 packages, Changfeng 8,000 packages, Runkang 2,000 packages, Yongda 2,200 packages, and Tonghe 1,800 packages. The purchases were Yuda 5,250 packages, Jinchang 2,000 packages, Daqing 1,150 packages, Hexing 12,300 packages, Changji 1,250 packages, Shenchang 1,250 packages, Changxing 1,800 packages, Renfeng 2,800 packages, Yida 1,600 packages, Dachangcheng 4,250 packages, Xiesheng 1,500 packages, Fukang 1,700 packages, and Xincheng 1,700 packages. The market prices are compared on the left.
