The Price Difference Between Cotton Yarn is Too Far; Cotton was Also Excited for a While; After All, There is Caution in Mind Due to the Harvest; The Later Market Has Long Liquidation 124

The cotton market turned up because the yarn market was soaring step by step, and the rise has reached the suspension, and the enthusiasm of people's hearts is rare in recent times, resulting in the cotton market, which is dependent on each other, to introduce a good situation. In fact, the price difference between cotton yarn is too far, so it is easy to cause multiple activities at the same time, and the spot cotton sales market is active.

Market Price Rose by One Yuan and Thirty-Five Cents

In the previous market of standard cotton, after the opening, the buying interest was slightly strong due to the continued rise in the yarn market, and each month rose by five or six corners. After the second market, it was still calm. However, most people's psychology is that the production is smooth, so they are bearish on the cotton market. Until the close, because the yarn market rose to the suspension level, people's hearts were agitated, and the price difference between cotton yarn was too far, causing a part to buy in. As a result, each month rose by one yuan to one yuan and four corners compared to the previous day's closing price. After the market opened in the afternoon, the buyers were more numerous because the yarn market was suspended, and the market was tighter. However, some of the longs liquidated, and the momentum of the second transaction was slightly flat. As a result, the near month rose by 1.2 corners compared to the closing price in the morning, and the distant month did not move. It was found that Dachangcheng sold 4,100 piculs, Tonghe 4,500 piculs, Tongji 7,900 piculs, Tongfu 2,600 piculs, Chengji 2,500 piculs, Shengyuan 3,200 piculs, Hengyi 4,100 piculs, Ju 4,500 piculs, Jinchang 2,700 piculs, Mingde 5,200 piculs, Ruida 4,600 piculs, Taichang 14,000 piculs, Runkang 3,400 piculs, Fukang 5,500 piculs, Yichang 5,600 piculs, Fengtai 2,000 piculs, and Yicheng 4,500 piculs. Factory Needs are Active, and Sales are Also Moving

The spot cotton consumption is launched, because the yarn market is rising, the factory needs are active, and the sources are 810 bales of Yao flower and 680 bales of Tong flower.

Standard Yarn Adds Special Margin; There is a Saying That There Will Be Another Increase Today 125

Standard yarn and cotton markets of Chinese yarn and cloth trading have been rising violently recently, so the stock exchange, in order to be safe, has decided that the new transactions made for December standard yarn will add a special margin of 8 yuan per package from the 1st, plus the previous 16 yuan, and December standard cotton will add a special margin of 3 yuan per dan, plus the previous 6 yuan, and the money is deposited in both accounts. According to market news today, standard yarn has a sharp increase and declares suspension. In the afternoon, there is still a stalemate and it has not been able to open. This serious situation is unheard of since the opening of the exchange. It is said that there are a lot of people in it, and the future situation is unpredictable. Probably from today (December 2), the special margin for cotton yarn will be increased by 16 yuan per package, and 6 yuan per dan for standard cotton, and the money is deposited in both accounts.

US Cotton Short Positions in the Near Term are Being Covered 126

Yesterday, the opening price of US cotton rose by four to nine pounds, and the short positions were covered in the near month. January and March were brought up by the buying of the December period by brokers and foreign merchants. The increase in hedging sales and long liquidation, and a part of the reaction, turned the market situation quiet before the close, and there were slight off-market transactions. The spot cotton market is quiet and firm, and the cloth market is more sluggish. At the close, the same industry bought the near month, and it was quite beautiful. It is estimated that spot goods rose by seven pounds, and futures rose by nine pounds to a drop of three pounds. British cotton spot goods rose by six points, futures rose by three or four points. Indian cotton exporters bought slightly, and were overturned by hedging sales. It is estimated that Pingguoer rose by 0.25 rupees, Aomura fell by 1 to 1.25 rupees, and Bailuoxi fell by 0.25 rupees. Although the price of pure gold in Yu City fell yesterday, the market was still stable due to the arrival of large households. Later, it gradually became tired because the buyers were satisfied. Securities and Bond Market: Morale is Weary and Incapable. Rumors of New Large Short Positions Appear. Result: Drop of Five to Six Jiao 129

Yesterday, the Chinese Securities Exchange and the government bond market continued to decline. Market conditions became increasingly sluggish. With the situation on the Sui frontier chaotic, morale was weary and incapable. Large bullish investors were selling off eagerly. Rumors spread that a certain large investor was taking a large short position by selling off large quantities of stock, which made market prices and sentiment weak. The selling trend was vigorous, and prices continued to fall. However, as retail investors gradually covered their short positions, the market situation stabilized slightly in the latter part of the day. However, the brewing situation and the bewildering nature of the on-stage situation indicate that drastic changes are still to come. The market's trajectory yesterday showed a clear inability to recover. However, at the beginning of the morning session, retail investors were eager to buy, and the "10.3" bond was also heavily purchased, causing market prices to rebound slightly by five fen to five jiao. However, in the second session, large investors such as "55.18.11" and "4" all sold off or released large quantities of stock. In particular, "45" sold huge amounts at every price point, causing a unified and sharp drop of 10 to 70 jiao. The afternoon session opened with a continuing downward trend, and morale was also bewildered and uncertain. "45.11.35" and other entities continued to offer a large number of chips, while "10.43.31" and others bought in quite a bit, causing market prices to fall again by a uniform small amount of five fen to six and a half jiao. Type A next month and Type B this month rose by five fen and one jiao, respectively. The closing market showed a slight firming, with many retail investors covering their short positions, and "5.10.54" and others also eagerly bought in, causing "Tong Wu Yi" and other bonds to rebound by five fen to three jiao. Type A next month fell by a small amount of one jiao. The overall result for the day was a uniform drop of five fen to six jiao. The total trading volume was 13,095,000 yuan. Banks Mostly Arbitraged Exchange Rates Yesterday 130

The exchange market yesterday saw rising exchange rates, a slight weakening of the US dollar, and a slight tightening of the shilling. In the morning, based on overseas telegrams, the London large and small bar quotations both narrowed by .0625. It was said that after the market closed, sellers reserved the right to add .0625 to the listed price. The New York silver market was unchanged, and the forward silver price in Montevideo was unchanged, or decreased by up to 1%. London gold fell by one penny, the British pound rose against the US dollar by .75, the British pound rose against the French franc by three pound coins, the US dollar rose against the British pound by .875, and the US dollar rose against the French franc by .9375. The Central Bank announced its listed prices, with both the British pound and the US dollar at par, and the Customs Gold Unit down by .02. The exchange market opened in the morning with the near-term forward price for the British pound at one shilling, two pence, and .5625, and the US dollar at 29.75 yuan. Compared to the previous closing, the British pound was at par and the US dollar weakened by .03125. After the opening, banks actively refrained from arbitrage. The Hong Kong and Shanghai Banking Corporation announced its listed prices, with both the British pound and the US dollar at par, as well as a silver parity tax of .0025, which had little impact. Later, banks engaged in forward selling and near-term buying, and Chinese merchants also engaged in swaps. Occasionally, banks dealt with each other and hovered around, and banks' appetites gradually became uncertain. At noon, the market was vague, and later the market inclined towards selling Cambodian currency and buying US dollars. Chinese firms sold, but the closing was flat, with the trend being a tightening of the British pound and a weakening of the US dollar. The closing selling prices for near-term forward British pounds were one shilling, two pence, .53125 and .5625, and for US dollars, 29.875 yuan and 29.75 yuan. Compared to the previous closing, the British pound tightened and the US dollar was at par. Chinese merchants slightly bought US dollars. The day's transactions are recorded below.

The British pound opened in the morning with a near-term selling price of one shilling, two pence, .5625. HSBC bought spot at .5625, favorable to HSBC at the same price for the same month, favorable to HSBC buying spot at .5625. Chartered Bank bought January at half a penny. Later in the market, Chartered Bank bought December at .5625. The closing selling prices were one shilling, two pence, .53125 and .5625, December at .53125, January at half a yuan, and February at .46875. The buying price was increased by .03125.

The US dollar opened in the morning with a near-term selling price of 29.75 yuan. Banque Franco-Chinoise bought spot at .75. Chartered Bank sold January at .625. Bank of China and Sin Hua Trust Savings Bank sold spot to Banque Franco-Chinoise at .75. Chartered Bank sold the first half of March at .5625. Great Britain bought the first half of January at .6875. Banque Belge pour l'Etranger (Extrême-Orient) favorable to East Asia Banking Corporation at the same price for the same month. Citibank sold spot at .75. Citibank bought December at .75. At noon, the near-term selling price was 29.75 yuan. Later in the market, the Farmers Bank sold to Chartered Bank February at .625. The Chekiang Industrial Bank sold spot to San Jin at .75. The closing selling prices were spot at 29.6875 yuan and .75, December at .6875, January at .625, and February at .5625. The buying price was increased by .0625.

Chiang Fang-chen and Wang Peng-sheng Returned to China on the Same Ship Yesterday, Arriving in Shanghai. Chiang Spoke of a World War Not Likely to Occur Soon, While Wang Said He Was Taking a Month's Leave to Attend to Private Matters. 131

Chiang Fang-chen

Mr. Chiang Fang-chen, who was previously ordered to go abroad to inspect military affairs, returned to China on the Japanese Empress ship of the Changxing Company at 2:30 PM yesterday, arriving in Shanghai. The ship docked at the Gonghexiang Wharf. Those who went to welcome him included Mr. Li Dachao, representative of Mayor Wu, Legislator Jian Youwen, Jianghai Customs Superintendent Zhu Changnian, Director Zhou Jue of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs' Shanghai Office, and Xue Dubi, Xu Xinliu, Yao Xijiu, and many others. After Mr. Chiang disembarked, he went directly to his private residence on Guofumen Road to rest. Mr. Chiang said when he met with reporters on the ship yesterday that he had visited Rome, Vienna, Berlin, Prague, London, New York, Washington, Los Angeles, San Francisco, and Tokyo, and had also observed the autumn exercises of Italy and Czechoslovakia. He originally planned to visit the Soviet Union on the way back, but he did not make the trip due to lack of time. In the past, people generally believed that the Blackshirts of Italy and the National Socialist Party of Germany adhered to the same doctrine. According to my investigation, the former's nature is cooperation, while the latter's nature is exclusion. The two are actually very different. As for the reason why Italy and Germany are close, it is based on mutual interests, just like the closeness between France and Russia. The current situation in Europe is extremely chaotic, so some people are worried that a second world war is about to break out. However, according to my observation, a world war will absolutely not occur, because the current disputes between countries are all trivial matters and there are no vital interests at stake.

Wang Peng-sheng

Mr. Wang Peng-sheng, Counselor of the Chinese Embassy in Japan, has requested leave to return to China to attend to matters and report on embassy affairs to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. He arrived in Shanghai on the Japanese Empress ship at 2:30 PM yesterday. The ship docked at the Gonghexiang Wharf. Director Zhou Jue of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs' Shanghai Office and Huang Bodu, Secretary of the Embassy in Japan, went to the port to welcome him. After Mr. Wang disembarked, he went to his residence to rest. He is scheduled to go to Beijing today to meet with Foreign Minister Zhang. According to Mr. Wang, speaking to the Central News Agency on the ship, he has been away from the country for a long time and has private matters at home that need to be handled, so he has requested leave to return to China and to report on embassy affairs to Foreign Minister Zhang on behalf of Ambassador Xu. Ambassador Xu originally planned to request leave to return to China, but he was unable to find the time due to the busy embassy affairs, so the date has not yet been determined. My vacation this time is for one month. After meeting with Foreign Minister Zhang, I will also meet with President Jiang and wait for instructions before determining the itinerary. Mr. Wang did not make detailed comments on the signing of the Japan-Germany Agreement and the recent negotiations between Japan and Italy, only saying that the embassy in Japan had heard of the Japan-Germany Agreement before it was signed and reported it to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. As for the content of the agreement, in addition to the officially announced content, the various rumors circulating are difficult to verify. Negotiations between Japan and Italy are ongoing, and it is difficult to say what the content will be. As for the future of Sino-Japanese negotiations, it depends on the attitude of the Japanese side.

Hu Qing-yu Set Sail Yesterday, Zhang Fu-liang to Depart on the 23rd, Xu Kai's Departure Date Not Yet Determined 132

Mr. Hu Qing-yu, the specialist sent by our country to the League of Nations to investigate administrative organization, set off abroad on the Soviet merchant ship "Northern" at 3:00 PM yesterday. The ship is scheduled to leave Shanghai at 5:00 AM this morning. At the same time, Guo Zefen, the new Consul to Moscow, is also on board. Mr. Hu is traveling to Vladivostok, where he will transfer to the Siberian Railway train and travel directly to Switzerland via the Soviet Union, Poland, and Germany, without stopping along the way, because he must arrive in Geneva before January 1 (i.e., New Year's Day) in accordance with the instructions of League of Nations Secretary-General Avenol. The investigation period is six months, and he will return to China next summer. Zhang Fu-liang of the Jiangxi Agricultural Experiment Station, who is also investigating cooperative enterprises, is also scheduled to depart on the German postal ship "Scharnhorst" on the 23rd of this month. As for Xu Kai, chief engineer of the Huai River Conservancy Committee, who is investigating water conservancy construction, the departure date has not yet been determined.

The British Embassy's Shanghai Office Opened Yesterday Afternoon. The British Ambassador Gave the Opening Speech. Mayor Wu and Others Went to Congratulate. 133

The British Embassy in China established an office in Shanghai on the fifth floor of the Jardine Matheson Building at 27 Bund, where the Commercial Counselor's Office, the Financial Advisor's Office, and the Export Credits Guarantee Department's representative office in China (representative Kirkpatrick, scheduled to arrive in China on the "Rawalpindi" on the 9th of this month) will be jointly located. The opening ceremony was held at 11:30 AM yesterday, presided over by the British Ambassador to China, Sir Hughe Knatchbull-Hugessen, who also held a tea party to receive Chinese and foreign officials for a tour. Those who attended to offer their congratulations included the Mayor of this city, Wu Tiecheng, Secretary Tang Shixuan, Songhu Garrison Commander Yang Hu, Secretary Sun Lüping, Director Zhou Jue of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs' Shanghai Office, as well as leaders from all walks of life, including Du Yuesheng, Wang Xiaolai, Yu Qiaqing, Zhou Zuomin, Qian Xinzhi, Xu Xinliu, and representatives of foreign embassies and consulates, as well as British residents, totaling more than 200 people. Ambassador Hugessen, accompanied by Commercial Counselor Beale, Financial Advisor Hall Patch, and Consul-General in Shanghai Brenan, warmly received the guests. At 12:00 PM, Ambassador Hugessen rose to give the opening speech, stating that the Embassy had specially established an office in Shanghai for the convenience of its work, combining the Commercial Counselor's Office, Financial Advisor's Office, and the Export Credits Guarantee Department representative in one office to achieve a division of labor and cooperation. He expressed his gratitude for the presence of guests from various countries. He then raised his glass in celebration, and the ceremony ended.

The Electrical Enterprise Public Bonds Were Drawn Yesterday Morning. Payments Will Begin at the End of the Month. 134

The twelfth redemption of the principal of the long-term Electrical Enterprise Public Bonds and the fifth redemption of the principal of the reissued Electrical Enterprise Public Bonds of the National Government's Construction Commission were drawn at the Bank Association on Hong Kong Road at 10:00 AM yesterday. Those present included Lin Kanghou, Chairman of the Fund Management Committee, Committee Members Yang J眉mei, Xu Dunkai of the Construction Commission, Zong Boxuan of the Ministry of Finance, Lin Jinyu of the Audit Department, Wu Weiru of the Bank Association, Zhang Dafu of the Money Dealers Association, Weng Gang of Siemens, Jin Jiyuan of the Central Bank, Cao Zhenzhao of the Bank of China, and Fan Xuexiang of the Bank of Communications, totaling more than 30 people.

Chairman's Report

Chairman Xu Dunkai reported that today is the date for drawing the principal of the long-term and short-term Electrical Enterprise Public Bonds and the reissued Electrical Enterprise Public Bonds. He expressed his honor at having everyone present to supervise. (1) The issue amount of the short-term Electrical Enterprise Public Bonds was 2.5 million yuan, with 1,925,000 yuan already redeemed, leaving 575,000 yuan outstanding. The eleventh redemption was 175,000 yuan, with interest of 23,000 yuan. (2) The issue amount of the long-term Electrical Enterprise Public Bonds was 1.5 million yuan, with 570,000 yuan already redeemed, leaving 930,000 yuan outstanding. The twelfth redemption was 60,000 yuan, with interest of 27,900 yuan. (3) The issue amount of the reissued Electrical Enterprise Public Bonds was 6 million yuan, with 720,000 yuan already redeemed, leaving 5,280,000 yuan outstanding. The fifth redemption was 180,000 yuan, with interest of 158,400 yuan. The total amount of principal redeemed above is 415,000 yuan, and the total amount of interest is 209,300 yuan. All payments are scheduled to begin at the end of December. He asked the supervisors to verify the lottery tickets and begin the drawing.

Winning Numbers

After the Chairman's report, the supervisors verified the lottery tickets and found them to be correct. The lottery was conducted by lottery personnel from the Bank of China, Bank of Communications and Zhejiang Industrial Bank. The winning numbers are recorded below: (1) Seven short-term Electrical Enterprise Public Bonds: No. 03, No. 49, No. 57, No. 612, No. 71, No. 90, No. 95. (2) Four long-term Electrical Enterprise Public Bonds: No. 20, No. 25, No. 61, No. 99. (3) Three reissued Electrical Enterprise Public Bonds: No. 54, No. 66, No. 72. The results will be announced by the Construction Commission's Fund Management Committee on the same day to inform the public.

Contribution to the Citizens, December 12, One Day of Exercise, the One-Day Exercise Promotion Association Held the Second Meeting Yesterday and Decided to Have All Circles Support the Movement for Relief in Suiyuan 135

The One-Day Income Contribution Movement Promotion Committee of this city held its second committee meeting at 3:00 PM yesterday. Those present included Tong Xingbai of the City Party Department, Li Dachao of the Municipal Government, Mi Jifang of the Social Affairs Bureau (representing Peng Quji), Yang Yongfu of the Garrison Command, Chu Yaohuan of the Local Association, Huang Zao Xiong of the Municipal Education Association, Sun Daosheng of the Journalists Association, Hu Fengxiang of the First Special District Citizens' Federation, Gong Jingdang of the Second Special District Citizens' Federation, Zhang Bingjun of the Lawyers Association, Zhu Yanggao of the Physicians Association, Zhang Zanchen of the National Medical Association, Ye Xianggao of the Federation of Trade Unions, Yu Zhenhui of the Municipal Farmers Association, and department directors Gu Shaoyan and Lu Baohua, totaling more than 10 people. The meeting was chaired by Tong Xingbai, with Gu Shaoyan as the recorder. First, the chairman read the resolutions of the previous meeting and reported on the progress of negotiations with banks for receiving funds. The representatives then reported on the progress of promoting the one-day exercise. Then the discussion of the proposals began. The results are as follows: (1) The Purchasing Machine Celebration Association sent a letter requesting that the promotion of the one-day exercise be carried out in the area of housing. Please review the proposal. (Resolution) The Association will do its best to support it and send a reply. (2) Propose to designate December 12 as Shanghai Citizens' One-Day Income Contribution Movement Day. Please review the proposed measures. (Resolution) Passed with revised measures. There were also temporary motions: (1) In the future, one-day income donations should be led by the various agencies and organizations participating in this association, and all donations must be submitted to the bank designated by this association. (2) Receipt books for one-day donations raised by the various agencies and organizations participating in this association will be uniformly printed by this association. (3) The newly established Secondary School Federation joins the committee. The above three motions were all passed as proposed. The meeting then adjourned.

China Merchants Bureau Employees

Employees of the state-run China Merchants Steam Navigation Company donated one day's salary, totaling 5,000 yuan, to support the soldiers defending Suiyuan Province in the harsh winter. They wired the money to Chairman Fu in Guihua (now Hohhot) through the China Enterprise Bank yesterday for the purpose of making cotton clothes. The text of their telegram to Chairman Fu is as follows: "To Chairman Fu of Guihua: The bandits invaded our borders, and thanks to you and your soldiers, braving the wind and snow, resisting bravely and recovering the fortress, the good news has spread and the people are in awe. However, the strong enemy still needs to be punished by heaven. It is hoped that you will sweep away the bandits and protect the frontier. All employees of this bureau have donated one day's salary, totaling 5,000 yuan, which is wired through the China Enterprise Bank for the purpose of making cotton clothes. Please accept it. Respectfully, Cai Zengmou, General Manager of the State-Run China Merchants Steam Navigation Company."

Mr. Wu Ruiyuan

Mr. Wu Ruiyuan, chairman of the Shanghai Yongda Bank, donated 5,000 yuan yesterday to comfort the soldiers at the front and telegraphed Chairman Fu, saying: "Urgent, to Chairman Fu of Suiyuan: The bandits' invasion of Suiyuan has angered the people. Fortunately, you are supervising the troops to suppress the bandits and protect our territory. We are thrilled to hear the news. Considering the soldiers fighting bravely in the harsh winter, we are sending 5,000 yuan through the Bank of China for comfort. Please acknowledge receipt. Respectfully, Wu Ruiyuan."

Tai Kang Employees

All staff and workers of Tai Kang Food Company held a one-day food rationing movement, saving a total of 115 yuan, which they entrusted to the Shenbao newspaper to forward to the soldiers at the front in Suiyuan.

Mr. Pang's Departure

Dr. Pang Jingzhou, specially dispatched by the Red Cross Society, took the night train to Beijing last night to coordinate medicines and materials with the Central Prevention and Treatment Office and the Ministry of Health, and then to Beiping to coordinate with major middle schools and the Peking Union Medical College to organize and train a rescue team. After the team is formed, he will lead the team to Datong and Suiyuan to carry out rescue work. At 8:30 last night, before his departure, Mr. Pang gave a speech on the situation after inspecting the war zone, saying:

Soliciting Winter Supplies

The Shanghai Rescue Work Promotion Association will convene leaders of the women's community and principals of various girls' schools at the Local Association this afternoon to discuss ways to solicit winter supplies. It is reported that items such as gloves, silk floss vests, and sanitary clothing are needed, but all new products are limited to domestic goods.

Donation of Woolen Socks

At the fourth regular meeting of the International Women's Fraternity Shanghai Branch on the 27th of last month, a dinner was held at Xinya on Nanjing Road. Considering that the soldiers on the Suiyuan border urgently needed winter clothing, the association first allocated 100 yuan from its existing membership fees to be used by the local YWCA to purchase 400 pairs of woolen socks and entrusted them to be sent directly to the front for use.

Donation of Woolen Vests

All teachers and students of the Shanghai Shangxian Tang Women's and Children's Hospital, Renhe Hospital, and Ruhe Advanced Mutual Aid Vocational School were moved by the hard work of the Suiyuan bandit suppression soldiers and enthusiastically donated money to purchase woolen yarn. Within a week, they knitted 120 vests and will send them to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce today to be forwarded to the front to comfort the soldiers at the front. Mrs. Ping Jinya of the outpatient department of Renhe Hospital donated 10 yuan to entrust the knitting of woolen vests to be included in the forwarding.

Comfort and Rescue Supplies to Begin Solicitation, Divided into Two Categories: Winter Protection and Medicine 136

The Comfort and Rescue Association organized by Wang Xiaolai and others, and signed by the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Local Association, and Red Cross Society, held its second standing committee meeting at 4:00 PM the day before yesterday. The Ministry of Railways' Materials Purchase Promissory Notes Were Issued Yesterday, with an Annual Interest Rate of 7%, Guaranteed by a Banking Consortium for Payment and Discount. Domestic Material Suppliers Are Willing to Accept and Promote Them. 138

According to the Xin Xin News Agency, in order to promote railway construction, encourage the production of domestic railway materials, and centralize purchases, the Ministry of Railways began issuing materials purchase promissory notes yesterday. To increase the credibility of the promissory notes, it was agreed that a banking consortium consisting of the Central Trust Bureau, and the Shanghai, Jincheng, Zhejiang Industrial, and Zhongnan banks would guarantee payment and handle discounts. The conditions are as follows: (1) The term of the promissory notes is one year from the date of issuance, with repayment due on the same day of the following year, plus interest at an annual rate of 7%. (2) The promissory notes will be issued over a period of twelve months. (3) The consortium will designate the Central Trust Bureau as its representative to endorse the promissory notes and guarantee payment on schedule. (4) The Ministry of Railways will entrust the Central Trust Bureau to accept the promissory notes when they mature and are due for payment of principal and interest. (5) The promissory notes will be made out to the payee and, before maturity, may be discounted or rediscounted by the holder or his assignee with the consortium's representative (Central Trust Bureau). The interest rate will be negotiated at any time. Therefore, the creditworthiness of the promissory notes is extremely reliable, and they will be freely circulated in the market in the future. Not only will the Ministry of Railways be able to purchase materials in large quantities based on its income and make successive orders from domestic merchants to implement various construction projects, but also domestic material suppliers and the banking consortium will receive considerable benefits. For the banking consortium, they can handle discounts and rediscounts at any time and use their funds. For the material suppliers, they can sell more materials. Although the purchase price is not in cash, they can discount the notes with the bank at any time before maturity. Therefore, domestic material suppliers are willing to accept and promote these promissory notes as much as possible to assist the government in building railways.

Capital Express to Begin Service on New Year's Day; Discounted Tickets Not Applicable; No Additional Cars Allowed

Preparations for the Capital Express on the Beijing-Shanghai Railway have been completed. It is scheduled to begin service on New Year's Day. The Traffic Departments of the two railways issued a notice yesterday stating: "It is hereby notified that the Ministry of Railways' decree Ye Zi No. 4543 of the 25th of this month, as per the decree of the Executive Yuan No. 6288 of October 24, 1936, and the decree of the National Government No. 788 of October 21, 1936, for compliance with the matter, as per the letter from the Secretariat of the Central Political Council of October 15, 1936, states: 'Approved the letter from the Executive Yuan, stating that the Ministry of Railways has submitted a proposal to run a high-speed special express train between Nanjing and Shanghai, named the Capital Express, from November this year, and requests that, following the precedent of the Shanghai-Ping special train, all public service travel passes, all discounts, free tickets, car passes, benefit tickets, preferential tickets, etc., except for round-trip tickets, shall not be applicable to the Capital Express. Furthermore, due to the reduced travel time and limited number of cars, additional flower cars shall not be added to this train in order to maintain revenue and show restraint. Please issue a circular and submit it to the Executive Yuan for compliance.' This matter was resolved and passed at the 282nd meeting of the Executive Yuan and sent to the Central Political Council for review and referral. We hereby sign and submit for review, etc." The matter was reported to the 24th meeting of the Central Political Council and approved for implementation. In addition to writing to the Central Executive Committee, we hereby record the case and attach a copy of the original letter, which is hereby delivered for review and compliance, and the Executive Yuan is notified, and its subordinates are instructed to comply, etc. Therefore, we must act accordingly. In addition to responding to and distributing the order, we hereby send the attached documents for compliance, and instruct your subordinates to comply, etc." Therefore, we must act accordingly and urgently instruct compliance. It is hereby notified to the heads of all sections, the chiefs of all traffic sections, the station masters of all stations, all ticket inspectors, all information desks, and all service desks, and copies are sent to all offices, departments, and passenger ticket management offices.

謝作民談　推進僑務　鼓勵僑胞回國投資　今後注重實施事項 142

Xie Zuomin Discusses Promoting Overseas Chinese Affairs, Encouraging Overseas Chinese to Invest in China, and Focusing on Implementation Matters in the Future

According to the Central News Agency, Xie Zuomin, member of the Central Committee and newly appointed Director of the Overseas Chinese Affairs Office in Guangzhou, arrived in Shanghai on the 30th from Nanjing to await passage south to take up his new post. Regarding the current situation of overseas Chinese affairs in Guangdong and the policies to be implemented in the future, Mr. Xie told a Central News Agency reporter as follows:

Situation of Overseas Chinese from Guangdong

Overseas Chinese from Guangdong have footprints all over the world. Not only are the economies of Guangzhou, Zhaoqing, Chaozhou, Meizhou, and Hainan largely dependent on remittances from overseas Chinese, but the economic construction and education of the entire Guangdong province also rely on the resources of overseas Chinese. In recent years, the political and construction progress in Guangdong has been slow. Furthermore, due to the impact of the recession felt by overseas Chinese, the flow of overseas resources has sharply decreased, and the hardships of the people have increased. This shows that the businesses of overseas Chinese from Guangdong have a significant impact on the livelihoods of the people in the province.

Encouraging Investment in China

Although overseas Chinese are in an environment of economic collapse, their foundations are solid and their economic strength can still be utilized. Therefore, the number of overseas Chinese returning to invest in China has not decreased compared to the past, and has even increased. Due to the changing situation of doing business abroad, overseas Chinese should be encouraged to invest in China. As for the capital that overseas Chinese move to China, the active capital overseas will be a problem that we must address, and we must plan and cultivate it. The method of cultivating resources should not only focus on managing individual assets from a positive perspective. We should guide overseas Chinese to mutually support all social organizations and adhere to the principles of modern economics.

Promoting Overseas Chinese Affairs in Guangdong

The situation of overseas Chinese abroad and the areas that should be focused on now have been described above. As for the promotion of overseas Chinese affairs in Guangdong in the future, based on my inspection in Guangdong last month, I believe that the following matters should be implemented: (1) "Guidance for Overseas Chinese Organizations": All social organizations should seek the welfare of the public. There are many overseas Chinese organizations in Guangdong. In order to promote the welfare of overseas Chinese, it is necessary to strengthen their forces and improve their organizations. Therefore, they should be rewarded or corrected and guided and assisted accordingly. (2) "Protecting Overseas Chinese Entering and Leaving the Country": Everyone knows the drawbacks of overseas Chinese entering and leaving the country. In the future, attention should be paid to improving passport issuance and visa procedures, investigating and requesting the abolition or modification of harsh regulations promulgated by governments in various places of residence, and preventing fraud in going abroad. (Regarding entry, we should fulfill our responsibility of guidance and protection, such as consulting with the customs to implement preferential measures for overseas Chinese entering the country, and notifying local officials in the hometowns of returning overseas Chinese to provide effective protection.) (3) "Guiding Overseas Chinese Children Returning to China for Education": The level of Chinese language proficiency of overseas Chinese children is generally low, which often affects their determination to return to China for further education. In the future, educational institutions at the provincial and municipal levels should be consulted to request the establishment of special classes to improve their Chinese language proficiency. (4) "Promoting Overseas Chinese Economic Organizations": The economic organizations of overseas Chinese must not remain scattered. Recognizing the modern economic environment and instilling economic knowledge are necessary. In particular, planned cooperation should be promoted, and experts should be hired to conduct research. (5) "Encouraging Overseas Chinese Investment": In the past, overseas Chinese often encountered obstacles and had no channels for investing in China. Therefore, in the future, relevant construction departments in the province should be consulted to investigate the needs of various places and the amount of capital required for businesses to be established in a certain place, and plans should be formulated at any time and announced to overseas Chinese through various means to encourage investment. (6) "Effective Relief for Unemployed Returning Overseas Chinese": In the past, unemployed overseas Chinese who returned to China were given travel expenses to return to their hometowns, but overseas Chinese have different living habits and work experience after being abroad for many years. After returning to their hometowns, they are still displaced and helpless. Therefore, giving money to return to their hometowns can only be a temporary measure and is not a fundamental solution. In the future, overseas Chinese investment projects should be used to accommodate unemployed returning overseas Chinese, and so on.

Difficulties in Forming Sino-Japanese Credit Loans; Yoshida Returns Crestfallen; Japanese Capitalists are Watching Due to Tense Sino-Japanese Relations 143

According to the Shenshi News Agency, Mr. Yoshida Seiji, Chairman of the Japanese Chamber of Commerce and Industry and Manager of the Shanghai Branch of Mitsubishi Bank, left Shanghai last month to return to Japan to attend the National Chamber of Commerce and Industry meeting. Having completed his mission, he arrived in Shanghai yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM aboard the Japanese mail ship "Shanghai Maru." According to rumors in business circles, Yoshida's trip to Japan was originally to request the Japanese authorities and influential figures in industry and commerce to proceed with Sino-Japanese credit loans in order to dump Japan's surplus goods. However, most prudent Japanese capitalists are adopting a wait-and-see attitude due to tense Sino-Japanese relations and the lack of guaranteed prospects, so the mission was unsuccessful, and Yoshida returned crestfallen.

Reduced Compensation for Undeveloped Tian (Reclaimed) Land; Half-Price Collection 145

The Third Tian (Reclaimed) Land Bureau of the Jiangsu Provincial Government recently received instructions from the provincial capital to extend the deadline for another three months for all Tian (Reclaimed) Land cases where land was leased before the 18th year of the Republic but not yet enclosed and developed, with compensation collected at half price. The announcement is recorded as follows: Jiangsu Province First Tian (Reclaimed) Land Bureau Announcement Sha Zi No. 2. Re: instructions from the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance, Sha Zi No. 20707, regarding this Bureau's submission on October 19th of the 25th year of the Republic for a half-price collection of compensation, proposing to extend the deadline for another three months to facilitate collection, requesting approval, which stated: "Noted. Regarding the proposal to extend the half-price collection of compensation for another three months to facilitate collection, etc., approval is granted to show consideration. In addition to forwarding to the First and Second Tian (Reclaimed) Land Bureaus and the counties of Ganyu, Yutai, Donghai, and Guanyun for unified compliance, you are to post a notice to inform all landholders and state on the notice that 'no further extensions will be granted' as a restriction. The draft of the notice and the start and end dates of the extension must be submitted to the Department for record and compliance. This order." Upon receipt of this, this Bureau notes that the previous extension of the deadline for half-price compensation coincided with the autumn harvest season in rural areas, preventing the preferential policy from reaching all households. Now that the autumn harvest has ended, and farmers are actively paying compensation, a request has been submitted to extend the deadline for three months to facilitate collection. In accordance with the aforementioned instructions, in addition to reporting and sending separate letters of instruction, it is imperative to post a notice to inform all: For all Tian (Reclaimed) Land cases where land was leased before May of the 18th year of the Republic but not yet enclosed and developed, half-price collection of land prices will still be permitted if payment is made before January 26th of the 26th year of the Republic. No further extensions will be granted. This matter is an exceptional act of consideration. It is essential not to delay or misunderstand. This notice is hereby issued on November 30th of the 25th year of the Republic of China.

Joint Winter Defense Begins in Military and Police Agencies in This City 148

The military and police agencies in this city routinely hold joint winter defense at the end of each year. However, due to the recent invasion of Suiyuan by bandits and puppet troops, it is being implemented earlier this year. The Municipal Public Security Bureau has begun inspections by land and water, and neighboring counties are conducting joint defense. Due to the sufficient local security in this city, kidnapping and theft cases have decreased compared to previous years. The details are recorded as follows:

Winter Defense Begins: In previous years, the winter defense period was scheduled to be held at the end of December. This year, it is the time of tension in Suiyuan border bandit suppression. It is feared that unscrupulous people will take the opportunity to spread rumors and disrupt local peace. Therefore, the military and police units, such as the Shanghai-Songhu Garrison Command, the Security Regiment, the Public Security Bureau, and the Security Committee, have planned to implement it earlier. The respective agencies have ordered their subordinates to follow the winter defense measures of previous years and begin winter defense.

Land and Water Inspections: The Municipal Public Security Bureau has ordered the police stations in each district to pay attention to inspecting suspicious pedestrians at any time. Since the flow of ships on waterways is more frequent, and it is easier for bandits to hide and traffic in illegal goods, special attention is paid to inspections. It is reported that the water patrol team has issued an order to its subordinate units to step up inspections of ships traveling to and from the Huangpu River, Suzhou Creek, and Wusong area. If anyone is found to be suspicious, they will be detained immediately.

Joint Defense in Neighboring Counties: The neighboring counties of Baoshan, Chuansha, Nanhui, Jiading, Songjiang, etc., in the suburbs of Shanghai, are jointly conducting winter defense with Shanghai to achieve better coordination of security forces. The method is that if a robbery or theft occurs at the junction of the city and the county, they will jointly investigate. If the crime scene belongs to Shanghai and the criminals are apprehended in the neighboring county, the case will be handled by Shanghai.

Decrease in Theft Cases: A reporter from the Dagong News Agency inquired with the competent authorities yesterday and learned that this year, due to the coordinated efforts of local security forces, the people are living in peace. The number of theft cases in the urban area has decreased by eight-tenths compared to last year. It is inevitable that poor and helpless people will take risks in the cold winter, but the police authorities have notified charitable organizations to provide as much relief and shelter as possible. In addition, with sufficient security, criminals have no way to succeed.

Continued Interception of Rice Boats; Qingpu and Yushan Permitted to Pass 150

The two counties of Pingyang and Yueqing in Zhejiang Province have also experienced the detention of rice boats leaving the province. The Shanghai Grain and Cereal Association has sent a letter to the local association, requesting that they telegraph the Zhejiang Provincial Government for their release. The original letter states: Respected Sirs, Previously, due to the prohibition of grain leaving Jiangsu and Zhejiang, this association submitted a letter to your association, which was presented to Chairman Huang of the Zhejiang Provincial Government, who replied that the prohibition of the export of food grains was purely to prevent leakage to the sea. If the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce has official proof, it can be transported. The city Chamber of Commerce handled the proof procedures, and at the same time, this association informed our colleagues that when purchasing and transporting food from Zhejiang Province, they must report to this association for verification and apply to the city Chamber of Commerce for a certificate, and at the same time, inform your association to report to the Zhejiang Provincial Government for record. Subsequently, at the 289th executive meeting of the Executive Yuan on the 24th of last month, it was resolved that food grains should be allowed to circulate freely, and the measures proposed by various provinces and cities to restrict the export of food grains were not in line with economic principles and the central government's overall management of food grains. Therefore, it seems that the counties of Zhejiang Province should no longer prevent export and should no longer use transportation permits or passports. However, it has recently been reported by the Jingtouzhen Rice Industry Association of Pingyang County that your colleagues Yu De, Qianfeng, and Weiyiheng sent partners here with a certificate from the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce to purchase and transport 10,000 bags of rice, but they were suddenly intercepted by the county government, detained and unable to leave. It is feared that the rice will become moldy. Please telegraph the Zhejiang Provincial Government to quickly order the Pingyang County Government to issue transportation permits so that they can be shipped, and Da Cheng and other colleagues have stated that the Yueqing County Government is in the same situation. Therefore, a letter has been prepared and sent to you. It is hoped that your association will investigate and telegraph the Zhejiang Provincial Government to quickly order the Pingyang and Yueqing County Governments to comply with the central government's resolutions, release the intercepted rice, and not obstruct transportation in the future, in order to comply with laws and regulations and benefit circulation. This is a matter of public interest. Respectfully addressed to Shanghai Local Association, Shanghai Grain, Cereal, Oil Cake Industry Association.

Jiading also Detains: A Large Number of Rice Boats

At 4:30 PM yesterday, a large number of more than 30 rice boats, which had been transported from Changshu to Shanghai for sale at the Xinzha Bridge in the northern part of the city, were suddenly intercepted by the police dispatched by the Jiading County Public Security Bureau near Wangmiao Temple in Jiading County and were not allowed to pass. The boat merchants sent representatives to Shanghai last night to report the detention to the North City Rice Store, the Hubei Rice Transportation Merchants Lianyi Association, and the Changshu Association, requesting negotiations. After discussing the solution last night, the association sent representatives to the Jiading County Government this morning to request their release.

Qingpu and Jinshan: Rice and Grain Allowed to Pass

More than 40 rice boats detained in Qingpu and Yushan counties in Jiangsu Province were released after various parties telegraphed the Jiangsu Provincial Government and the county chambers of commerce and rice industry groups negotiated. The detained rice will be temporarily stored in the stores, and will be released after the provincial order. The rice and grain currently being transported through the border will be allowed to circulate as usual and will no longer be detained.

Tax on Re-Export of Miscellaneous Grains and Peanuts: Two-Year Extension of Exemption; Miscellaneous Grain Industry Submits Document to the Ministry of Finance 152

The Shanghai Miscellaneous Grain and Oil Cake Industry Association yesterday submitted a request to the Ministry of Finance and the Customs Administration for a two-year extension of the exemption from the re-export tax on miscellaneous grains, peanuts, peanut oil, and peanut kernels. The original submission stated: It was previously investigated that the Jiaohai Customs was ordered to exempt the re-export tax on domestically transported peanuts and native products for two years starting from April 21 of the previous year. The association's colleagues Shen Shouting and Yuan Tang carefully observed that the peanuts operated in Shanghai are mostly from Shandong, Henan, Anhui, and Jiangsu. If re-export tax is exempted, the products from the above-mentioned places will be transported to Haizhou by the Longhai Railway for export, transferring to Qingdao, Shanghai will be greatly affected. It is requested that the association send a letter to the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, earnestly requesting the Ministry (your department) to follow the precedent of Qingdao and grant a unified exemption. In response, the (Customs Administration) (your department) approved on November 22 of the 23rd year that what was said was indeed true. It has been reported to the Ministry of Finance for approval, and it has been specially approved to exempt the re-export tax on peanuts, peanut kernels, and peanut oil transported from Shanghai to various domestic ports. In addition to ordering the General Tax Office to transfer the order to the Jianghai Customs for compliance, the starting date of the exemption should be reported for record. This approval, and on December 3 of the same year, the Jianghai Customs Superintendent Tax Office jointly issued Announcement No. 1405, stating that the re-export tax on the aforementioned goods will be exempted for two years from November 29 of this year. Merchants should be notified, etc., on record. It is now investigated that the exemption period for the re-export tax on peanuts, peanut oil, and peanut kernels transported from Qingdao to China will expire on April 21 of this year, and the Ministry (Ministry of Finance) has approved a two-year extension. The exemption period for the re-export tax on peanuts, peanut oil, and peanut kernels transported from Shanghai to China will also expire on November 29 of this year. Jianghai Customs will restore taxation on the re-export of the aforementioned goods. The association believes that the situation in Qingdao and Shanghai is the same. The extension of the tax exemption needs to be followed as a precedent. A document is specially prepared and submitted to your department for review and transfer (Ministry of Finance for review) and still follows the precedent of Qingdao, granting a two-year extension of the tax exemption to benefit commerce. We are eagerly awaiting orders. Respectfully presented to Minister of Finance Kong and Director of Customs Zheng Lai.

City Police Bai Yunfeng: Pursues Gray-Clad Thieves; Chases from Panjia Street into the Concession; Police and Thieves Exchange Fire for More Than Ten Shots 155

At about 2:30 AM yesterday morning, three men dressed in gray cloth robes and blue cloth shirts and pants were seen wandering back and forth in Panjia Lane in the city. Their actions were suspicious, and they were noticed by police officer Bai Yunfeng of the No. 4 post at the entrance of the lane, who took precautions by secretly drawing his service pistol and hiding it in his sleeve. Before long, one of the robbers wearing a gray cloth robe approached the post, a few feet away, suddenly drew a gun and shouted, forbidding movement. At this point, the robbers' intentions were revealed. Officer Bai was agile, immediately dodged, and loaded his gun. Then, the robbers fired two shots in a row, fortunately missing. The police also fired back. The two sides exchanged fire for more than ten shots. The robbers were no match and turned around and fled into the French Concession Jixiang Street, running north. Officer Bai chased after them, blowing his whistle. Neighboring officers from the No. 5 post and the Cross-Border Police assisted in the pursuit and fired warning shots, chasing them all the way to a branch lane near Avenue Edward VII. It was late at night, and it was dark and difficult to distinguish, and they eventually escaped.

Drowning and Hanging 157

The Shanghai District Court Procuratorate reported two cases yesterday, one of drowning and one of hanging, according to reports from the water patrol police. Chief Prosecutor Mei and other prosecutors were dispatched to the Nanshi Lifesaving Bureau to conduct examinations in accordance with the law. The two cases are recorded separately below:

Drowning by Jumping into River: At about 10:00 AM yesterday, the Hengqing small wheel of the Yitaixing Coal Wharf was carrying passengers to the junction of Yangjingbangkou Heping Shenpumian. Suddenly, an old man, about fifty years old, dressed in a wool blend camel hair coat, resembling someone from the upper class, jumped into the river unnoticed. Although he was rescued by a sampan boatman and reported to the police and sent to Renji Hospital for treatment, he died on the way to the hospital. His body was sent to the Nanshi Lifesaving Bureau, and the water patrol police reported to the District Court. The court dispatched a prosecutor in the afternoon to conduct an examination. As there were no relatives, the body was given a coffin by the charity organization for burial.

Hanging from Shed Roof: The Taikoo Company's Kuai Du small wheel was docked overnight at Pier No. 2 of the Pudong Huatong Wharf. At 12:00 PM last night, a young man of about 24 or 25 years old, dressed in a blue cloth long gown, white cloth blue striped intelligentsia shirt, and black cloth pants, was found hanging from the iron frame of the shed roof. The post police were immediately notified, and the water patrol police were informed and reported to the District Court, which also dispatched a prosecutor to conduct an examination in the afternoon. The Bureau provided a coffin and buried him in the public cemetery, awaiting family members to claim the body.

Russian Bravely Captures Thief; Tragically Shot and Killed by Bandit; Another Russian Fortunately Unharmed; Police Hope Victims Will Testify 159

At 12:20 PM yesterday, a fashionable young woman was riding in a chartered car on Route Lafayette near Rue Constant in the French Concession, traveling from east to west. Suddenly, two robbers riding bicycles came rushing past the left side of the chartered car and snatched the handbag from the young woman's hand in the car. One of the robbers took out a pistol and threatened her, forcing the driver of the chartered car to flee into a nearby store. Unexpectedly, two Russians happened to be on the side of the road at the time and witnessed the woman being robbed. They immediately bravely ran across the road to chase the two robbers. One of the Russians knocked down one of the robbers' bicycles, but the robber turned around and fired two shots. One bullet hit the Russian in the neck, and he immediately fell to the ground and died. The other bullet grazed the hair of the second Russian, but fortunately, he was not injured. The two robbers were able to calmly get on their bicycles and escape towards Route Lallemand. The robbed woman and the driver of the chartered car also left without a trace. After the nearby police arrived and reported to the police station, the captain immediately dispatched a large number of Chinese and Western detectives to investigate. It was learned that the Russian who was shot and killed was named Li Amini, 36 years old, formerly worked at the British-owned Water Company, and currently works at the Church on Avenue Joffre. The body was immediately transported to the Westerner's morgue on Route Trolard to await examination. The other Russian's name is Fei Yinaosi. The police are currently strictly hunting down the perpetrators and hope that the young woman and the driver of the chartered car who were robbed at the time will quickly turn themselves in to the police station and describe the situation at the time to facilitate the police's investigation. The victim of the robbery has no responsibility for this case.

Avoiding a Repeat of Last Winter's Dagu Ice Navigation Calamity: Customs Sets Sailing Procedures, Specifies Lightship Equipment and Ice Signals, Effective December 1st 161

To ensure safe passage for ships sailing the North China route, as winter approaches and the river is about to freeze, and in light of the ice-bound conditions at Dagu last winter, the Customs has specially set forth winter sailing procedures to avoid a repeat of last year's disaster. These procedures took effect yesterday (December 1st) and are recorded below:

Lightship Equipment

Around December 1st this year, the Dagu Lightship will be withdrawn. However, during the winter period, the winter lightship "Haiming" will be stationed in its original location as a replacement. This lightship will display a black ball during the day, and at night, it will use a white quick-flashing light that flashes once every twelve seconds (i.e., bright for one and a half seconds, off for ten and a half seconds). In clear weather, it can be seen within a radius of 18.52 kilometers (10 nautical miles). If the "Haiming" lightship's lighting equipment malfunctions, the ship will use its searchlight as a substitute, flashing it towards the sea every ten seconds. Once the equipment is repaired, it will return to its original state. In dull weather or heavy fog, if approaching ships can hear it, it will strike the gong once every minute. In inclement weather, the ship may move away and return to its original location when the weather improves. When necessary, it may also leave its original location during the day to take on supplies. However, if the weather is good at that time, the Customs transport vessel "Tianshun" will be dispatched as a substitute. The "Tianshun" transport vessel will display a black ball on its foremast, its hull is white, and its smokestack is light yellow. The "Haiming" lightship's smokestack remains white for identification purposes.

Municipal Federation Issues Letters of Negotiation: Interest Should Be Paid on Electricity and Water Deposits 162

The First Special District Municipal Federation yesterday issued letters to the Shanghai Electric Power Company and the Waterworks Company, stating, "Regarding the commercial practice in this city of paying interest on deposits and guarantees received from others, the Shanghai Electric Power Company and the Waterworks Company collect deposits from users. If these deposits are mortgaged with the respective company's stocks, interest can still be collected according to the face value of the stocks upon maturity. However, most of the deposits paid by citizens are in cash, and their nature is the same as mortgages and credit. The income of each company from cash deposits is very large, but we have not seen each company paying interest, which is a deprivation and encroachment on the interests of others, and also violates legal principles. This matter was brought up for discussion at the meeting yesterday, and it was resolved to write to your association, requesting that you uphold justice and strive to negotiate with each company reasonably to protect the rights of citizens. We have recorded the case and request your investigation and prompt negotiation to safeguard the interests of citizens." It is believed that user deposits are originally for credit and guarantee purposes, and interest should be paid. Otherwise, the company will find it difficult to avoid the suspicion of encroaching on the interests of others. In view of the above, we hereby request your company to promptly stipulate a method for paying interest on deposits in order to demonstrate fairness and justice."

Ice Conditions

During the ice season, the icebreaker "Qingling" stationed in Dagu (radio call sign XNEI) will broadcast QST signals by radio at 10:30 AM and 5:30 PM daily (which can be received by all radio stations) on a wavelength of 600 meters, reporting on ice conditions at the Dagu estuary, the time and height of the last high tide, and all urgent news related to weather and navigation. However, ship captains should refrain from transmitting radio signals daily between 10:00 AM and 11:00 AM, and between 4:00 PM and 5:00 PM, to avoid interfering with the icebreaker's communication with its supervisory authorities. If ships have any inquiries about ice conditions, they may contact the icebreaker by radio on a wavelength of 600 meters at 9:00 AM, 12:00 noon, 3:00 PM, and 6:00 PM daily, and they will be answered promptly. If the icebreaker leaves its original location and goes out to sea, someone should be on duty every hour to answer inquiries, but telegrams not related to ice conditions will not be answered. When ships arrive in Tianjin or Tanggu, the ship captains should immediately report the ice conditions encountered en route to the port authorities for reference and cooperation. Furthermore, ship captains should also use the following signals to inform passing ships of the ice conditions they have encountered along the way, so as to alert them:

Ice Signals

The applicable signals are listed below: (1) Signals for ice on the Dagu River: Signal: no ice; Signal 2: thin ice (navigation is still easy); Signal 1.3: thin ice (navigation will gradually become difficult); Signal 3: thick ice (navigation is difficult); Signal 3.2: thick ice (navigation is difficult, but there is a tendency to become easier); Signal 3.4: thick ice (navigation is difficult, but there is a tendency to become more difficult); Signal 4: thick ice (navigation is very difficult); Signal 4.3: thick ice (navigation is very difficult, but there is a tendency to become easier); Signal 4.5: solid ice (navigation is impossible). (2) Signals for ice in Bohai Bay: Signal 6: no ice; Signal 7: thin ice (navigation is still easy); Signal 7.8: thin ice (navigation is gradually becoming difficult); Signal 8: thick ice (navigation is difficult); Signal 8.7: thick ice (navigation is difficult, but there is a tendency to become easier); Signal 8.9: thick ice (navigation is difficult, but there is a tendency to become more difficult); Signal 9: thick ice (navigation is very difficult); Signal 9.8: thick ice (navigation is very difficult, but there is a tendency to become easier); Signal 9.10: solid ice (navigation is very difficult or may be impossible); Signal 10: solid ice (navigation is impossible).

Cipher Discovered on Hongkou Utility Poles: Police Are Investigating 163

The Shanghai Japanese Daily, translated by the Foreign News Agency, reports that Japanese residents in the Zhabei and Hongkou areas have recently felt uneasy again. On the night of the 29th, a policeman from the Hongkou Police Station, while patrolling near the Japanese Telegraph Bureau on Tianji Road, discovered a white "×" mark on a street corner utility pole. The white powder was very fresh and seemed to have been painted recently, which he found strange. Upon further investigation of the adjacent utility poles, he found direction-indicating " " arrows. At the street corners or intersections in the direction of the arrows, there were "×" or " " marks. Growing more suspicious, he reported it to the Hongkou Police Station. The police station dispatched personnel to investigate various locations within its jurisdiction, and found that in the densely populated Japanese areas of Seward Road, Tiantong Road, Wusong Road, and Haining Road, there were these white marks on utility poles everywhere. The police station is paying close attention and will conduct further investigation.

Madam Hardoon Sued: Hearing Held Yesterday, No Result Yet 164

The Evening Post reports that after the death of Shanghai businessman Hardoon, who left his entire estate to his wife, Rachel Hardoon, a relative of Hardoon's recently hired lawyers Harris and Fischmann to sue the widow in the British Supreme Court for China. The plaintiff claims that the deceased Hardoon was an Iraqi national, and according to Iraqi law, a widow may not receive more than one-quarter of the total value of the estate. The remaining assets should be divided among the deceased's relatives. The case was heard in court this morning (the 1st) by the Supreme Court. The defendant hired lawyers Puddefoot, Lighte, and Bardesley to defend her. The defendant's lawyers did not admit that the deceased was an Iraqi national, but only admitted that the deceased's father was born in Baghdad and that the deceased had legally become a British citizen. The plaintiff's lawyers refuted this, claiming that the deceased was only under British protection and was not a British citizen. After much debate, there was no result. The relationship between the plaintiff and the deceased was not clarified. The plaintiff only stated that he was entrusted by all the deceased's relatives to file the lawsuit in Shanghai.

Female Teacher's Lawsuit Allowed to be Withdrawn 175

Lin Jun, 38 years old, a native of Chuansha and the principal of Jingping Middle School on Father Lao Shen Road, and Jiusan Primary School on Fangjia Wooden Bridge in Zhabei, was recently sued by Shen Fuzhen, a female English teacher from Suzhou who was dismissed from Jingping Middle School, for the crime of seduction and disrupting public morals. After the court opened hearings several times, the plaintiff never appeared. Only the defendant's lawyer appeared in court and said that the case had been settled out of court and requested a postponement. The plaintiff then filed a request with the court to withdraw the lawsuit. The judge verified the bizarre circumstances of the case and ordered that the defendant and the lawyer who wrote the complaint on behalf of the plaintiff be summoned to court to clarify the situation. Yesterday, Sun Peng, a judge from the Special Second Court, continued the hearing in the first criminal court. The defendant Lin Jun, accompanied by his defense lawyer, and the lawyer You Zhi, who was commissioned by the plaintiff to write the complaint, appeared in court. You claimed that he was not in court as the plaintiff's agent, but as a witness. The lawyer had not been released from the plaintiff's commission. At first, Shen Fuzhen asked someone to represent her in commissioning the lawyer to handle the lawsuit. He then ordered Shen to come in person to confirm the commission. The next day, the representative said that Shen was ill in bed and presented a draft of the complaint written by Shen herself, with Shen's seal on it, and asked him to proceed with the lawsuit on her behalf. Later, the lawyer went with the representative to see Shen Fuzhen in person. Shen said, "Will I be able to not appear in court in the future?" The lawyer replied according to the law, "If the court summons you, you must appear in court, you cannot refuse." Shen then said that if she had to appear in court, she would not proceed with the lawsuit. Later, Shen filed a request to withdraw the lawsuit, which the lawyer did not know about. If the court needs to summon Shen in person for questioning, Shen lives at No. 24 Back Street, Zhouzhuang, Suzhou. He also presented Shen's handwritten draft complaint and a stamped power of attorney. After the court verified that the handwriting of the draft and the seal were consistent with the withdrawal request, it declared that the lawsuit would be allowed to be withdrawn and ruled that the case would not be accepted.

The fire quickly broke through the roof, and the strong northwest wind caused it to spread to the neighboring houses, including the upper floor of the Fuyuanyuan barbershop at No. 105, the upper floor of the Longxing restaurant at No. 103, and the upper floor of the Maoxinglong porridge shop at No. 101. Fortunately, the French Concession Fire Brigade had received the alert early and rushed fire trucks to the scene to extinguish the fire. It was extinguished at around 1:00 AM this morning. As a result, the upper floors of four houses were destroyed, and the losses were heavy. The arsonist fled after the fire started and is currently being pursued.

After members of the Blood Soul Anti-Traitor Group, such as Tu Dongcai, were arrested by Chinese and Western detectives from the Lao Zha Police Station and sent to the First Special District Court for sentencing, the internal organization and main members of the group were revealed. The Special First Court issued arrest warrants for the group's main figures, Zhang Zilian, Jiang Zhonghe, Ren Jinping, Wang Jingzhi, and Wang Zixiang. Jiang Zhonghe was later arrested, and Ren Jinping surrendered himself. The court approved their release on bail of 3,000 yuan each. Li Mingde's Involvement with a Dancing Girl Creates Repeated Commotion: Wife Accuses Him of Adultery; Dancing Girl Accuses Him of Seduction 179

Li Mingde, thirty years old, son of Li Hongfa, a comprador for the Osaka branch of the Japanese Mitsubishi Company, and a native of Ningbo, is already married to a Mrs. Cao. Because of his family's wealth, Li is a spoiled young man and currently a student at Guanghua University. Dance halls and theaters are naturally the places where modern young people seek entertainment, and Li Mingde is no exception. Therefore, in 1933, he met a local dancing girl, Miss Fan (nineteen years old this year). It was love at first sight, and they spent every evening together. Their mutual affection led to a romance, clinging to each other like glue, vowing eternal love. Li Mingde then advanced to seeking cohabitation, falsely claiming he was unmarried. Thus, in May 1934, they established a small family in the French Concession of Mucun Street, living as husband and wife. The crystallization of their love occurred in February 1935. Mrs Cao filed a private suit in the Criminal Court. When summoned for questioning, Li Mingde admitted to all the facts with Miss Fan, but claimed, "Our love is very deep. I believe Miss Fan would never sue me; she is completely being manipulated and instigated by her brother-in-law. But I swear I love her, even if I am sanctioned by law and imprisoned, I will always love her." His tone was as if, after the birth of their two little angels, their love for each other became even deeper. Therefore, Li Mingde even wrote a contract for Miss Fan, stating that if he abandoned her halfway, he would pay her 50,000 yuan in living expenses. Unexpectedly, their love affair was fraught with obstacles. Their secret was discovered by Li's wife, Mrs. Cao, who brought the lovebirds to court, accusing them of adultery. Later, through the intervention of relatives, Mrs. Cao softened her stance, considering the marital relationship, and withdrew the lawsuit. The relatives and Li Mingde himself thought that one husband and two wives would allow the family to enjoy the bliss forever. Unexpectedly, just as Mrs. Cao's commotion subsided, Miss Fan suddenly refused to be a minor concubine and hired a lawyer to accuse Li Mingde of using deceit to make her mistakenly believe they were married, and of seducing a woman under twenty years old. She asked the local court to facilitate this amorous affair. Miss Fan repeatedly stated in court that she no longer loved Li Mingde. The judge verified that Miss Fan was under the legal age of twenty and therefore could not file a private suit. He ruled that the private suit was inadmissible and transferred the case to the prosecutor's office for investigation. Prosecutor Mei Yinji interrogated them, and both parties repeated their previous statements. The prosecutor instructed Li Mingde to post bail and await public prosecution according to the law.

Page 17

Detectives Discover Goods-Swindling Criminal During Hotel Inspection: Fraudulently Establishes Company to Swindle Silk, Pays with Checks and Flees, Apprentice's Panic Reveals Case 180

Dai Ganrong from Hangzhou recently fraudulently established a cotton yarn and silk brokerage firm named "Xiechangxiang" at 4 Renzhi Lane, North Sichuan Road. He hired Xu Yongquan from Shaoxing as the accountant and Dai Changben from Taizhou as the apprentice. Around 9 AM on the 23rd of last month, Dai Ganrong went to Wanlong Silk Store at 10, Lane 360, Beijing Road, and selected twenty pieces of silk of various colors, worth 514 yuan, from the clerk, Chen Zubei from Shaoxing. He ordered them to be sent to Xiechangxiang for payment and hurried away. The silk store sent the apprentice, Wang Shourong, and a porter in a hired cart to deliver the goods in full.

Accountant Xu Yongquan paid apprentice Wang with a check from Zikang Bank on Tianjin Road, No. 114, dated the 27th, and Wang took it back to his boss, Wang Mingjiu. Wang Mingjiu ordered someone to cash the check at Zikang, but they were told that the check was a forgery and that they did not do business with Xiechangxiang, so it was returned. Silk store clerk Chen Zubei and apprentice Wang

rushed to Xiechangxiang to find Dai Ganrong, but the shop's

doors were tightly closed

and the place was empty. They realized it was a swindling scheme and reported it to the General Police Station for arrest. The detectives from the Jiaru Road Police Station, Shao Fan, Liang Muyang, Yang Xinzheng, Xu Yongyuan, and Dong Qingquan, together with Western detectives, inspected hotels along East Jiaxing Road around 8 PM the day before yesterday

for bandits

in hiding. At Room 57 in the Shangyuan Hotel, they found Dai Changben, the apprentice from Xiechangxiang. When he saw the Chinese and Western detectives, he panicked. When questioned, he stammered. In a leather suitcase, they found a package of the stolen silk and forty-one pawn tickets. Under strict questioning, he confessed to the scheme to swindle the Jiulong Silk Store. In time, Dai Ganrong, his wife Mrs. Li, his employee Xu Yongquan, and a suspect from Taizhou, Wang Ziwu,

arrived one after another

and were arrested. Six more pieces of stolen silk were also seized. Eight pieces were said to be at a dyeing shop for changing colors. The five men and women were taken to the police station and detained separately. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. Attorney Zhang Shizhu from the Public Works Department detailed the case and requested an extension

to investigate another case.

He also stated that a forged check was kept in the Central Police Station and would be presented to the court when the trial opened. According to Chen Zubei and Wang Shourong, the employees of Jiulong Silk Store, who testified about the incident, Judge Zhong Qing questioned the defendants, but their statements were evasive. They claimed that the boss was a Mr. Li who was on the run. Therefore, the judge ordered them to be remanded in custody and postponed the hearing for seven days for further review.

Truth About the Shooting of a Police Sergeant at the Xinzao Sub-Bureau 181

It was previously reported that Li Huai, the duty police sergeant at the Xinzao Public Security Sub-Bureau in Zhabei, was suddenly shot the night before last, and that the details had been recorded. It is now known that the incident occurred when a policeman from the upstairs patrol squad returned to the bureau after inspecting pedestrians. A policeman named Zhang Yunjun was in the bedroom, carelessly unloading bullets from a Mauser pistol when it accidentally discharged. The bullet shot through the floor. The duty office was located there, and at that time, the police sergeant Li

was washing his face by the tea table near the wall, causing the bullet to strike his lower right waist. He immediately fell to the ground in pain. Fortunately, the bullet had passed through the floorboard and had lost much of its force, so it did not pass through his body. The sub-bureau chief Liao Jiongran and other officers arrived quickly

and immediately ordered Police Sergeant Li to be sent to Baolong Hospital in the Concession for treatment. The injury was not critical and

did not pose a threat to his life. It has already been

communicated that Chief Liao has sent a letter to the

hospital, requesting the

doctors to treat him with care, and all medical expenses would be borne by the sub-bureau. As for the policeman Zhang Yunjun who caused the accident, he was immediately detained and yesterday was sent to the Public Security Bureau for questioning.

Wang Changfu Sues His Wife for Divorce 182

Wang Changfu from Yancheng, thirty-nine years old, works as a driver at the tram company. His wife, Mrs. Wang Lin, is also thirty-nine years old. They both live at 14 Fuxi Lane, Zhongde Road, Zhabei. He claimed that she did not cherish her honor in old

age. She claimed to be working in a factory, but she was avoiding her husband's supervision and spending all day and night outside, committing adultery without shame. She even

committed adultery with her maternal uncle, Zhang Hua, and the latter was recently detained in your court's detention center for theft. She visited him frequently and Zhang sent her two love letters from the detention center, filled with obscene and sickening words, even calling himself "your beloved brother Zhang Huasan." His eighteen-year-old eldest son received these letters and gave them to me. Using "brother" instead of "uncle," her adulterous

affair is fully exposed. Zhang Huasan is a malicious person, and I fear he will resort to violence. Therefore, I request permission for a divorce. Yesterday, Judge Yuan

held a hearing. The plaintiff stated as above and presented the love letters

as evidence. The case had also gone through the criminal court, and after her husband's aunt testified against her, she was acquitted. At the same time, he and his mistress beat me up, and the court fined them each ten yuan. She now requests that the court order her to live with her husband.
