Purchasing a Bail Bond and Getting Hit by a Tram: Xu Zhixun's Life in Danger 183

Xu Zhixun from Hubei, thirty-one years old, was originally a farmer in his hometown. He recently came to Shanghai and went to the Pig Bristle Factory at 6 next to the local government office in Nanshi to visit his cousin Xu Zhigui and his brother. The two brothers quickly became companions on outings. The day before yesterday, Xu Zhigui went to a gambling den in Yuqing Lane, West Xinjiao Street, in the French Concession and was arrested by the police. Yesterday, he was sent to the Eighth Criminal Court of the Second Special District Court for trial. Xu Zhixun learned of this and went to the Second Special District Court to visit his cousin Xu Zhigui yesterday morning. He then learned that Zhigui could be released on bail. At 11:30 AM, Zhixun held four yuan in cash and rushed out of the Second Special District Court, intending to purchase a bail bond at the office across the street. In his haste, he ran across the road, when a Route 17 tram No. 309, driven by driver Renzhi, was driving from west to east. As it approached the Second Special District Court, Xu ran across the road, and the driver was unable to stop in time, causing Xu to be violently knocked to the ground. The tram's headlight and a five-centimeter-thick piece of glass shattered. Xu was knocked down, bleeding from his nose and mouth, and immediately fainted. The patrolmen checked and, along with the tram driver, rescued Xu and hired a car to send him to Guangci Hospital for treatment. They then took the driver to the police station for questioning. The driver

drove the car and was driving along. It was heard that Xu had thick glass embedded in his eye socket and was seriously injured, and that his life was in danger.

Duan Yilin Fills Out Ten Pages of Confessions at the Police Station: Explains Each Item of Confiscated Documents; Recounts the Course of the Japanese Spinning Factory Strike; Case Continues in the First Special District Court Yesterday 185

Duan Yilin, a clerk in the workshop of the Second Factory of the Japanese-owned Shanghai Spinning Factory in Yangshupu Road, was arrested by the police on suspicion of inciting others to strike. Many documents were confiscated, and he was sent to the First Special District Court for detention. All of this has been reported in this newspaper. Yesterday was the date for the continued hearing of this case. Judge Zhan Liangce opened the criminal court for interrogation. Attorney Jiang Baolian from the police station charged him under Article 304 of the Criminal Code, stating that Duan had personally written a detailed confession in the police station, totaling over ten pages and thousands of words. In his confession, in addition to explaining each item of the confiscated documents, he also admitted that he was a leading figure in the strike at the Japanese spinning factory and a key member of the East District Representative Loyalty Association of the Shanghai Textile Industry Mutual Aid Society. The work of the Mutual Aid Society was to print various documents related to the strike, while the Loyalty Association assisted the workers financially. For example, when the police arrested a criminal, they found many rice tickets on his person. This person was a member of the Loyalty Association, and the rice tickets were used to provide for the striking workers. However, Duan absolutely denied any involvement with the National Salvation Association. Duan also confessed that the strike leader Yang Xiaoxian had not yet been apprehended, but Yang's brother, Yang Xiaozhong, had already been arrested and sentenced to fifty days of detention by your court. After Judge Zhan questioned Duan, he ordered Duan to be remanded in custody and postponed the hearing again.

Sichuan Store Gives Away Bamboo Woven Toys 191

The Sichuan Store in this city specializes in Sichuan white fungus and all kinds of Sichuan local products, and has been in business for almost ten years. Every year, there is a commemorative price reduction to thank customers. The store, with its years of reputation, refuses to raise prices and sell cheap products. Instead, it purchased a variety of exquisitely handmade bamboo woven toys from Sichuan, which are delicate and can be used for children to play with or as containers. Enthusiastic people who want to assist and comfort the soldiers on the front lines can go to purchase it. Letters to the Editor 196

Dear Editor,

In your newspaper on the date of this month, there was a new section about the donation of the Customs Finance Section colleagues to support the soldiers on the front lines. With a total of 76 yuan, it read: "Except for a few, most people have exceeded their one-day income." This sentence is very inconsistent with the facts. The largest donation was from Mr. Chen of the same section who donated 20 silver dollars. This sum only amounts to half of Mr. Chen's daily income. It should be changed to: "Except for Jia Chengkai, who donated 5 silver dollars, everyone else donated an amount less than their daily income." The person who announced this statement was Jia. He could not distinguish whether it was a large or a small number. It seems he was not satisfied with those who donated less, and he arbitrarily overturned the truth. It is not known to him that those who donated less have younger brothers and sisters who are in university or middle school, and children in elementary school. This family relies on daily income to survive. At the time of the front line support movement, they are also part of the donation. However, within Jia's household, you cannot find anyone like that. Therefore, "those who donated more were still those who donated less. The minority changed to the majority." To the editor of Shen Bao, Fang Xiyue of the Customs Finance Section, December 1.

Dear Editor, Your newspaper's report of the postponed questioning of Ye Fukan's case contained the phrase, "but because Wang Hanqing had already reached a settlement outside of court," which caused great surprise. Various shocking reports that defamed and accused Wang Hanqing of fraud, previously appeared in your newspaper, and you corrected them. Now there is such a rumor again, which must be due to other motives. (And the court only summoned him for the second day of the hearing, there was no postponement.) Please correct it according to law to ensure accuracy. Ye Fukan

Dear Editor, In your local news section of your newspaper for the past two days, there were reports of "Using Heavy Measures to Hold Back Grain, Cao Du Rice Boats Stop" and "Changshu Local Office Requests a Crackdown on Heavy Measures to Hold Back Grain." These reports are completely false. Cao Du Rice Shops do not have an agreement with city rice shops. There is only the heavy measure. There is no instance where both measures were used at the same time. The truth is there and can be confirmed. As for saying that "an apprentice robbed the scoop," it is a false accusation. In addition to questioning the Changshu Local Office, we are afraid that there will be misunderstandings from the outside world. We are writing to request a serious correction. We hope you will publish this. The Hengyi Public, Yuanchengchang, Dingtai, Zhang Xiehe and other rice shops of Caojiadu, December 1, 25th year.

Shen Bao National Goods Special Publication

A Word of Contribution

Responding to Women Using National Products 199

— Yang An

The Women's National Products Consumption Association, organized by women in Shanghai, was established on November 11th. Since then, the first board meeting was held to discuss all aspects of the implementation plan. The major points are as follows:

(1) Contacting the principals of various girls' schools to request them to lead all female students to join the Women's National Products Consumption Association, and mobilizing all female students to persuade their families to consistently use national products.

(2) Contacting various national product factories to convey opinions and findings on household consumption, and providing practical feedback on any dissatisfaction with the products, hoping for gradual improvement. At the same time, any dissatisfaction with the service attitude of the staff in national product companies should also be brought to their attention for improvement.

(3) Contacting various sectors of society to solicit their efforts in promoting national products. Also, it is hoped that if there are any goods commonly used by women for which there are no domestic products, they will quickly find ways to manufacture them themselves, so as to prevent the outflow of profits.

(4) Sending Ms. Lu Lihua to various provinces such as Anhui, Jiangxi, Hubei, and Hunan to encourage the organization of national product consumption associations for liaison purposes. Since the announcement of this proposal, it has been reported that there has been a great response in various places. The principals of various girls' schools have also begun organizing national product consumption groups and promotion groups in their schools. As a result of Ms. Lu Lihua's visits to various provinces, national product consumption associations have been organized everywhere with great momentum, and the future looks very promising. We believe that the Women's National Products Consumption Association should pay more attention to the following two matters:

First, investigate the sales of national products in various regions, the opinions of local women on national products, and whether national products are sufficient, or whether there are only foreign goods available for purchase and no national products.

Second, personally contact various factories to conduct on-site research on the products, identifying which parts should be improved, which parts should be modified, and which parts should be paid attention to. Detailed and meticulous work must be done to conduct thorough discussions.

Winter and National Products 200

— Ba Ling

Winter is coming, winter is the last season of the year; it is also the season when most people's purchasing power is at its strongest. Purchasing cotton-woven clothing, preparing winter tonics, and planning winter gifts are mostly planned and prepared in advance at the beginning of this winter season. Therefore, when winter begins to arrive, if comrades who are enthusiastic about promoting national products can take advantage of this opportunity to promote the consumption of national products to their relatives and friends, the effect will definitely be much greater than writing a few articles on national products. This can be asserted.

I believe that when most people are planning to prepare winter supplies, we might as well introduce them to some genuine and authentic national products and ask them to try them out. If they are satisfied with them, honestly and unreservedly ask them to purchase more and also persuade their relatives and friends to promote and use them together. If there are any shortcomings after trying them out, they may also be asked to contribute them as much as possible, so as to serve as a basis for improvement. For example, when purchasing sanitary shirts, we can introduce them to the Goose Brand sanitary shirts from the Wuhe Weaving Factory and the Duke Brand sanitary shirts from the Jinglun Shirt and Socks Factory, which are not only soft and comfortable, but also durable. For snow cream, we can introduce them to the Butterfly Cream from the Family Industry Cooperative, the Times Cream from the China Chemical Industry Cooperative, and the White Snow from the Yonghe Industrial Company. If you need to purchase overshoes because of the rainy weather in winter, then you can introduce them to the Double Coin Brand from the Greater China Rubber Factory and the Warrior Brand and Wanli Brand from the Zhenggtai Rubber Factory, as well as the Jian Gu Brand from the Yisheng Rubber Factory, and so on. We can really give a wide variety of examples, introducing some famous national product factories' well-known products to our relatives and friends as a timely reference.

In short, there is no need to say too much nonsense. The facts are now in front of us, and winter has arrived. How to promote this winter national product movement? How to enable the national product industry to achieve substantial progress in this winter season with strong purchasing power? This is a question worthy of study at present. At the same time, it is also what people who care about the national product movement should pay close attention to. As the saying goes: "We should not recall the past, nor dream of the future, but firmly grasp the present, because the present is the most precious."

Promoting national products is indeed also about grasping the reality. May everyone work hard to persuade and not let go of this promising winter national product movement.

After the Establishment of the Women's National Products Consumption Association 201

— Yu Yushu

The Shanghai Women's National Products Consumption Association, which has been in preparation for many years, was officially launched after holding an inauguration ceremony on the afternoon of November 11th.

Many people have said before that promoting national products must start with our women compatriots. Therefore, after the National Products Year for Women, the China National Products Production and Sales Association initiated the invitation of women compatriots to organize a Women's National Products Consumption Association during the New Year's social event this spring. At that time, many people volunteered to join. In the past six months, with the efforts of female national product visitors, the number of members has been increasing day by day, and now there are nearly a thousand members.

Although there are many national product organizations in Shanghai, this is the first women's organization. Therefore, I would like to offer some personal opinions after the establishment of the association:

First, we must practice what we preach. Our compatriots have a common problem, which is that they embrace a perfunctory and careless attitude in everything. Someone asks me to join an organization, and I agree vaguely because it is difficult to refuse due to face, but afterwards I never get close to that organization and become a "honorary member" forever. We should correct this attitude, especially after joining this Women's National Products Consumption Association, it is not just a matter of hanging up a name and signing a voluntary statement! You must know that using national products is our obligation, and to put it plainly, it can also be regarded as our right. We are Chinese people and cannot give up the right to use Chinese goods. After I swear to join this association, I should abide by the association's creed. I myself need to use national products and promote them, so that the entire family also uses national products. Most of the members who join the association are housewives. If they can all abide by this creed, they can quickly make everything used in each family purely national products.

Second, we should expand the organization. The current number of members is obviously insufficient in terms of both quality and quantity. There is a Women's National Products Consumption Association in Xi'an, which has more than 30,000 members. Compared with the population ratio, we should try our best to develop it. Moreover, the scope of future recruitment should be expanded to include general housewives, shop assistants, factory workers, and other consumer groups. The more widespread the publicity and the more people who participate, the more effective it will be.

Furthermore, from the perspective of the Women's National Products Consumption Association, in the entire national product cause, they are still only standing on the consumer side. If they can more actively promote production work, so that the national product industry can be developed and innovated, that would be what the author hopes for!

When the Weather is Cool but Not Cold, A Proposal to Compatriots 202

— Wang Shouqiu

Time flies, and in the blink of an eye, it is autumn again! In the present "cool but not cold weather", everyone is busy preparing autumn and winter clothes. Of course, the manuscripts published in this journal naturally belong to national products. My manuscript is naturally no exception.

The slogan of promoting national products has been shouted for three or four years, and the banner of the National Products Year has also been raised for several years. However, what are our achievements? Although it cannot be said that there are absolutely none, upon detailed inspection, it is quite pitiful. Especially now, goods from imported brands have filled the market, and a certain national product is very active. Looking back at national products, they are full of lifelessness. Everything is really worrying.

No matter what we do, we must be based on the spirit of perseverance. Promoting national products is naturally the same. Therefore, we must continue to work hard. Now, it is already autumn! Among our compatriots, many want to prepare autumn or winter clothes. I hope everyone will make a determination and not forget the four characters of promoting national products when preparing autumn and winter clothes. Of course, the amount of national products we promote is very small. However, gathering the power of the majority can be very substantial. For example, among the 400 million people in China, 40 million people prepare autumn and winter clothes, and calculating an average of one yuan per person, it would be 40 million yuan. If all of them buy national products, then 40 million yuan can be used for the development of national product manufacturers. If all of them buy imported goods, then this 40 million yuan will become a leakage of the country's wealth, and national product manufacturers will suffer a major blow. This is the meaning of "many grains of sand form a tower" and "many fox furs make a robe."

Compatriots! I hope everyone will not create a leakage of even one cent. I am sincerely praying.

Puppet 206

— Wo Fo

Speaking of "puppet," one cannot help but feel quite heartbroken, because there are too many Chinese people with puppet-like qualities. At the same time, the influence of puppets on the country cannot be considered small. However, it is very pitiful! Those who are acting as puppets still think they are carrying out promotions and are grateful to tears.

Puppets are called "big stage palace戏" or "托偶" by northerners, and "本人头戏" by southerners. As for the invention of Chinese puppets, it dates back to the Zhou Muwang era more than 900 years before the Christian era. In the book Liezi, it is recorded that Yan Shi made clay figures, dressed them in human clothes, and held them to dance. The puppets made eyes at the left and right of the king, and the king did not know it was a play, and was very angry and wanted to kill him. Yan Shi was afraid and quickly destroyed the clay figures, which were made of cinnabar glue and lacquer. Also, when Emperor Gaozu of Han heard Chen Ping's plan, he carved wooden beauties to dance on the siege walls to show off to the Guan clan. The Guan clan was afraid of losing favor, and ordered Modun to lift the siege, so Emperor Gaozu was able to escape. From the Tang to the Song dynasties, the types of puppets became increasingly prosperous, including suspended silk puppets, wire puppets, gunpowder puppets, rod puppets, meat puppets, and water puppets. Various names were almost as developed as actors and dramas. Also, according to various records, puppets were also called 窟儡子, also known as 魁　子, also known as 郭秃, also known as 郭公. In the puppet shows of the Tang Dynasty, there was also Guo Lang. In short, they were nothing more than things for people to play with.

As for puppet poems, what I can know is one by Tang Minghuang and one by Han Nizhou's clan son. Tang Minghuang's poem was written for Li Fuguo when he moved to the Western Palace. The poem is: "Carved wood and pulled silk to make an old man, chicken skin and crane hair are the same as real, after playing for a while, there is nothing, still a dream in life." Song Ren Pang Pingying's Tan Souzai: "Han Nizhou held a banquet in Nan Garden, and his clan son Pan Yuan was there. During the banquet, someone offered a silk puppet to be a clay figure carrying a small child, named Yingchun Huang Pang. Han wished his clan son, you can write poetry, you can sing. He immediately accepted the order and sang a poem: 'Stepping on the void and playing with spring, one person must settle on his head, suddenly the thread breaks in the child's hand, and the flesh and blood become dust on the road.' Han was very unhappy." These two poems are excellent. "'After playing for a while, there is nothing, still a dream in life.' 'Suddenly the thread breaks in the child's hand, and the flesh and blood become dust on the road.' I would like to say to the 'meat puppets' who are willing to be child emperors and recognize thieves as fathers, let's review these words three times.

Mr. Dunlop 207

— Zhu Ying

Mr. Dunlop is one of my colleagues. He is fat, has a round face, and is always smiling. Anyone who meets him feels very approachable. But after interacting with him a few times, everyone has to shake their heads at him.

Mr. Dunlop's surname is not Dunlop, and his name is not Lu Pu. The name Dunlop was given to him by his colleagues because Mr. Dunlop has a very special habit. As long as there is a little bit of a small advantage, even if he gets glared at or ridiculed, he doesn't care at all. Therefore, everyone rushed to call him Dunlop, saying that his skin is as thick as a Dunlop car tire. When he first became famous, he was a little shy about this nickname and didn't dare to accept it, but now, he takes it for granted.

Mr. Dunlop always has an empty cigarette case all year round, but within the six or seven hours of office work every day, he has to smoke at least ten cigarettes. The only source of his cigarettes is to ask his colleagues for them with a thick face. Fortunately, there are nearly twenty colleagues. In addition to those who do not smoke, on average, each person gives him a few, which is enough. But if someone refuses to give him one, he will make a ghost face and say, "Dunlop can touch Goodyear." Because Goodyear is also a type of tire, everyone is afraid of having a strange title, so they finally give him one to end the matter. Sometimes, when he has nowhere to get a cigarette, he goes to ask the director questions, and in the end, he always grabs one from the cigarette can on the director's desk. Recently, the director also knows his trick, so when he sees him coming up, he always gives him one first, and then, leaving behind a few names, he leaves with a cigarette in his mouth.

All year round, he doesn't spend a penny to buy snacks. If other colleagues buy crab shell yellow or fried steamed buns, he always makes sure to get a bite. Starting last year, we organized a monthly dinner party, held once a month. At that time, we invited Dunlop to join, but he shook his head and said, "It's not interesting, I won't join." But when we have a dinner party, he always comes as an uninvited guest. Later, we always secretly try not to let him know the date and location, but sometimes, he still finds out and comes on time, eating and drinking for free with laughter and talk, not stopping until he is completely drunk. If there is a festival in someone's home, then naturally he will not be absent.

Recently, the tea room attendant A'er also calls him Mr. Dunlop, because he has pestered him to go to the amusement park twice and drink once. In the end, he always patted his butt and thanked him, watching A'er take out his wallet to pay.

News brief: Huang Yao's "Cow Nose" has long been popular around the world and has received high praise. Schools in various parts of the country have also adopted it as teaching material. The author has now registered with the government and is implementing the creative initiative of the "Cow Nose Society" to create tools for "education" and "art." The first product is a small notepad, four volumes in one set, each volume selling for three cents. Students are given preferential treatment, and they only need to enclose a one-cent stamp to receive a trial set. Please send a letter to the Credit Service Cooperative, No. 30, Tongan Lane, Yongxing Road, Shanghai.

People are Always at the Mercy of Time 208

—

The World's Largest Telescope 209

— Te

The Mount Palomar Ridge in California is now building an observatory. The large telescope used in the observatory has a mirror surface of 200 inches and costs 2 million US dollars. Looking at the sky through this telescope, the distance can be increased by twice as much as all existing telescopes. It can discover stars and nebulae that have never been imagined before, and it can make the moon feel closer to the earth, as if it were only 2,500 miles away. The glass blank used for the mirror is like a large round block of butter, weighing ten tons. In order to grind this glass into a mirror surface, a special machine was built. Its form is like a record player, weighing fifty tons, and the machine has two giant arms, like the curved handle that inserts the needle on a record player. Instead of inserting a needle, it is inlaid with a cast iron disc, with a diameter from four feet to nine feet, which rubs against the glass. Needless to say, the position for the record is the large piece of glass. The machine has been running since May of this year, and has barely stopped until now. It will probably take another twenty months to complete. The machine is placed in an optical laboratory with heavy curtains, no sunlight, no dust, and clean air. Skilled craftsmen who grind glass and great literary figures take care of this work. The glass must be ground into a parabolic concave surface, with the center about four inches lower than the sides. The polishing work is extremely fine. If there is a defect of one millionth of an inch, it can be detected and immediately eliminated. The machine rotates once every minute, which seems to be very slow. In fact, this project began in 1928. It was not until December 1934 that 104 ladles of molten glass were used to cast a large glass blank at a temperature one-fifth of that of the sun. The blank was left as a whole for a year, and the temperature gradually decreased and cooled. Then, it was transported by special train from Corning, New York to Pasadena, where the machine was polished. It is expected to be completed by 1940, forming a telescope. When polishing, it is necessary to be very careful not to have any spots or lines. The large piece of glass can be erected to check for spots or whether it is flat. During the inspection, extremely strong light must be used, and shot from a tube onto the mirror surface. If the mirror surface is absolutely flat, then the mirror will be as bright as a full moon. If there are uneven spots on the mirror surface, then dark spots will appear, and then that point must be polished again. Before the completion of three years of work, more than three tons of glass must be removed. The main material used for polishing is emery and gemstone slurry. Experts cannot estimate how much slurry is needed. While the polishing machine is turning slowly, other preparations are being carried out step by step. It is expected that the mirror can be used around 1940, and then the stars that can be seen in the sky can be one or two times farther than they are now. The site for building the observatory has already been purchased on the 6,126-foot Mount Palomar Ridge. First, a road must be built from the foot of the mountain to the ridge to transport materials. An airfield will also be built to accommodate scientists from the California Institute of Technology and other groups. In addition, US$1 million will be used to build houses to house the auxiliary machinery and all the instruments that have been built at the California Institute of Technology. The frame of the telescope weighs 850 tons and is currently being manufactured in Philadelphia. Among them is a 55-foot-long lattice metal tube, in which a scientist can sit to use the telescope, like a bird in a cage. After the meteorological observatory is completed in the future, it can peek into the stars in the sky that people have never seen before. The estimated cost is between US$6 million and US$10 million. Most of it has already been raised from the Rockefeller Foundation, a coal oil tycoon.

Changing Nest Luanfeng 210

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter 8: Swearing Allegiance with a Glass of Water, Grieving in a Green Light; Hooking Gold and Promising Love with Red Beans

There was a letter with the note, gently narrating, all about sending this ring. Among them was a passage:

"We have always been friends in righteousness, so the items given to each other may as well be regarded as gifts given by friends in righteousness, so as to set off the spirit and preserve the memory. There is no need to regard it with worldly eyes and have any scruples."

These few dozen words can be said to completely free Guo Qi from the situation he imagined. Because of this, it is definitely Meng Lan's tone. He gave the gold ring out of his own volition, there is no doubt about it. With this letter, Guo Qi pondered for one night, and felt that he could not get rid of the words "friends in righteousness", which was a kind of depression. But he didn't know what Meng Lan's true meaning was, and what he had with him, and he couldn't say that the words "friends in righteousness" were not what he had to say. Therefore, on the surface, he would never deny the words "friends in righteousness". Early the next morning, he took down a small rosewood box from the bookshelf, opened it, and there were many beloved small items inside. The best was a small rectangular brocade box, only the size of a thumb. Inside, there were two red beans padded with white velvet. There was a piece of glass on the brocade box, so you could see it without opening the lid. On the bottom of the box, in small print, was written an ancient poem, "This thing is the most lovesick." He picked it up and played with it for a long time, and also found a Western-style envelope to put it in along with the box. Then, he wrote a line from the Book of Songs on it, "Forever and ever, for the good." After he had dealt with it properly, he wrote another letter, with the envelope clearly marked "Respectfully entrust to deliver to your friend, Mr. Mingshan." He also put a lot of thought into the two words "Mingshan". He used Mingshan to allude to Yougu. From the two words Yougu, he then involved the word Lan. This was a meaning that only people inside the circle could understand. He put both envelopes on the desk, and he felt very at ease. He only hoped that Miss Li, the messenger, would arrive. After sitting quietly for a while, looking at the shadow of the sun outside the window, he carefully read the letter he had received last night again, and said to himself: "It says clearly that he will come this morning." But then he turned around and thought to himself, the so-called morning includes everything before twelve o'clock, and it is still only ten o'clock now, of course there is still a while. So he suppressed his impatience, picked up a book and read it, and ground an inkstone of ink and wrote two large calligraphy characters. After all this was done, the clock in the hall naturally struck twelve times. The morning appointment had been missed. Whether this Miss Li would be able to send out his two lovesick beans on his behalf was unknown. (105)

Local Customs and Anecdotes

West Lake Double Marvels 211

— Shen Zhen

The beauty of Ming Sheng lies not in the lake but in the stream, not in the water but in the mountain. I have explored it thoroughly, and only after a long time did I begin to grasp its essence. Circling the lake once, admiring the first hints of green melting into the dawn and the gentle rising of spring mist, I thought I had seen it all. Later, climbing Taoguang Peak and scaling Wansong Peak, looking down at the Qiantang River like a ribbon and the secluded bays like snails, I again thought I had seen it all. After numerous visits, I gradually grew tired of it and secretly wondered at the mediocrity of what I had once thought beautiful. So, I roamed to the farthest reaches, determined to explore its wonders. But even with Cloud Dwelling Temple, Nine Creeks, Misty Glow, and the Three Bamboo Temples, my footsteps reaching far and wide, I found nothing. Then one day, passing through Li'an, the openness and remoteness, the quietness, held a different charm. Initially, I didn't pay much attention, but a refreshing breeze suddenly passed by, opening my eyes wide, and I began to explore it with my staff. I felt an overwhelming surge of emerald green, my eyebrows almost transforming, mountain birds singing occasionally, and a zither playing on the rocks. It was secluded but not desolate, containing but not revealing, occupying the harmony of the land and capturing the interest in stillness. Gradually, I found it extraordinary and decided to stay for a day to enjoy it. At noon, the rooster was silent, the monks didn't chant, the fading sun came and went, the empty mountain was silent, and the fun of the recluse was in the painting. The trees wrote rhymes, the mountain breeze passed through the creek, weary feathers shook their clothes, and a slight coolness arose on the sleeves. The fun was in the evening. At night, the clock struck once, the clear chimes moved slowly, the fragrant chanting was like rain, and the faint sound of the stream was heard. The fun was on the pillow. When the birds woke me up in the morning, the first rays of sunlight leaked through the pillow, the overnight mist gradually dissipated, the vibrant green seemed to flow, the morning chants echoed around the beams, and the dreams of yesterday left no trace. The fun of the morning was different from usual. I felt happy and content, reluctantly leaving, with the lingering taste in my thoughts. Its beauty is like Li Geng looking at a stele, only after repeated contemplation does one truly understand. I regretted not being able to live there freely, staying for three days. Like suddenly obtaining a bright pearl, a wonderful interest suddenly arose. I rented a small boat, untied the loose wooden [unclear word], and followed the creek road out. For dozens of miles, there was no break. The wonderful view was complete. The green cicadas were a thousand heads, and the yellow shirts were on both banks. The bridges were bustling, and the oranges were lively. The frost-covered forests were scattered with red, and the wild fields were covered in purple. The persimmons were clustered, and the chestnuts were bunched. After entering another ten miles, the ultimate beauty was the reed catkins. This was West Creek. The creek was known for its reed catkins. For ten miles around the water, east, west, north, and south, the chaotic streams were like a spider web, and the veins were all connected. There was no creek without reeds. When the boat entered its borders, front, back, left, and right, it twisted and turned, drawing the oar into the deep waves, and the first and last were all reed catkins. Silver light fluttered, greeting with bows and seeing off with deep bows. Leaning on the side of the boat, I admired the view. The accumulated colors flowed, and the softness was lovely. My hair and eyebrows were white, and the dust on my clothes was all gone. I moored at Autumn Snow Hermitage, which was the most beautiful place in West Creek. Climbing the stairs, I tapped my fingers, and hundreds of poets from past dynasties in Zhejiang were worshiped. The arrangement was simple and elegant, and the cold interest was pleasant. Opening the window, I saw ten thousand reeds reflecting each other, a piece of auspicious silver, a snowy scene. Within ten miles, there was no hidden shadow. Looking at each one, the color changed, and the width was different. A monk asked about the road, cooked creek water to make tea, and offered cakes to alleviate hunger, quite attentive. Staying overnight would be a great thing, but unfortunately, the dust of the world urged dreams, and I regretted not being able to stay a little longer. Going out to the Interwoven Reeds Hermitage, the land turned secluded and remote. The couplets in the building were extremely exquisite, with unique and wonderful meanings. Looking at the reed catkins, one could also exhaust their appearance. There was also an ancient ancestral hall in the creek, worshiping Fan Xie, the great master. The two virtuous men were old friends, and their actions were open and unrestrained, not just known as children of poetry. The walls of the hall were engraved with several verses of Da Zong's poem mourning Fan Xie. The couplet "The eastern suburbs are cold after the vegetable-picking festival, the southern country is sad at the silkworm-gathering spring" was once widely circulated, admired as the concluding verse of the poem mourning Fan Xie. I could imagine the depth of the two men's righteousness. Hundreds of years later, stroking their handwriting, I couldn't help but feel a strange emotion. Turning to Liu Xia, I climbed the Flower Mound. The bamboo path was high and deep, quiet and contemplative, only hearing the sound of footsteps mixed with the bamboo's rustling, the stillness becoming solemn. There was a pavilion on the ridge, with an old woman serving tea. Sitting for a long time, I forgot my fatigue. Feeling a little hungry, I ate a few salted chicken eggs and returned. The beauty of the creek could be compared to Li'an. Although the mountains and waters were different, their beauty was not inferior. This is why I know that the beauty of Ming Sheng should be sought outside the lake and mountains.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talk

Italy and Japan Form Another Alliance 212

— Wen

I remember that just two days ago, the Italian ambassador to China still stated that rumors of an agreement between Italy and Japan, with Japan recognizing Italy's annexation of Abyssinia and Italy recognizing Manchukuo as an exchange condition, were completely "rumors." But the Italy-Japan agreement has actually been realized. This has left the Italian ambassador in an awkward position, only able to tell reporters: "I don't know if this is the case at all, and I have nothing to say," and so on. For a long time, I have been preparing to muster the courage to admire Mussolini and Hitler. But reality always makes it difficult for me to do so. For example, after reading Hitler's "Mein Kampf," which says that Chinese people are an inferior race, I thought that I would not be honored to serve the highest authority among the superior races as a slave. This chilled half of my heart for admiring Hitler. Now, I have discovered that Germany and Italy, personally arranged by Hitler and Mussolini, are on very friendly terms with those who are invading us. Aren't the friends of our enemies also our enemies? Even the most foolish and hopeless person would not willingly feed tigers and wolves with their own flesh. This chilled another half of the heart I had prepared to admire the two heroes, Mussolini and Hitler. The remaining thoughts are still to guard the door, outside which a group of tigers and wolves are staring at me!

Of course, when a tiger and wolf wants to enter your door, it will never wear a frightening fur coat, but will be disguised. For example, if our "friendly nation" wants to announce its "Royal Way" in our country, spreading the grace of the "Manchu Empire" to the heads of every Chinese person, it would be frightening to say so honestly. Therefore, the substitute slogans are "friendship," "cooperation," and joint defense against something. They say that this is a great plan of a Royal Way state to establish peace in East Asia and pacify the world, and that the Chinese people must "thoroughly understand" it. Recently, they have also been saying: "The Inner Mongolian army's operations in Suiyuan are due to the increasing oppression by the Chinese Communist Party and Chinese military groups closely related to Communist organizations, so they have no choice but to defend themselves in this way. The goal of Inner Mongolia coincides with the urgent national policy of Japan and Manchukuo. The Japanese military authorities hope for the success of Inner Mongolia, so they cannot be indifferent to incidents that would harm the security and order of Manchukuo or Bolshevize the entire territory of China" (Joint announcement by Manchukuo and the Kwantung Army on the military situation in eastern Suiyuan). According to this announcement, the logic is: all those who oppose Manchukuo are Communists; and the Chinese troops currently fighting against the Inner Mongolian army are all members of the Chinese Communist Party or have close ties to the Communist Party. Therefore, if all of China opposes Manchukuo, it proves that China has been completely Bolshevized; and if all of China is not to be Bolshevized, in other words, the entire territory of China must be "Royal Way-ized." To rephrase it, opposing Manchukuo and Bolshevization are two sides of the same coin, so if you don't want Bolshevization, the only option is for all of China to submit to the Royal Way" and support the Japanese Empire—this is not a literary game, but that is indeed what our "friendly nation" means.

The Japan-Italy alliance has once again revealed the true face of the expansionists. According to the above "either/or" explanation for China, under the Japan-Italy-Germany alliance, China's fate is: either be their dog or be a ghost under their knife—there is no other way!

Is there really no other way?

At Sea 213

— Zhu Mingxia

Wind and Rain Chapter 1

When the horizon could be faintly seen, the sky began to darken. In the faintly visible western sky, black clouds were busily floating, like a suddenly chaotic crowd, bumping and squeezing each other.

The captain, who was in charge of the helm, firmly grasped the rudder handle, and the boat sailed straight southwest. "There will be a storm tonight," he thought.

He stared at the sky, his experienced eyes seeming to see through the wind and clouds as if they were tangible things. The sea was relatively calm.

A seagull spread its white wings and swept past the side of the boat, giving him a glimpse of brightness.

Page 20

. He looked at the滔滔 waters, testing the speed of the boat: then looked at the chaotic black clouds, estimating the speed of the wind. He was very confident that the boat would reach the shore first, and then the wind would strike.

The waves seemed to be even calmer than before, and the sails were taking the full force of the favorable wind, slightly bulging like a belly full of food. But he felt dissatisfied. He released the rudder and turned the winch holding the sail a few times, so that the sail stretched straight to the masthead, very upright, and the boat sailed faster.

Several young sailors were lying on the deck, happily talking about women, and sometimes even laughing out loud. The captain was reluctant to break their happy atmosphere, and忍着 not to tell them what was about to happen.

The sky was completely black, and the black clouds covered half of the sky. Only a few large stars on the eastern side of the sea were twinkling vigorously. - They were getting closer to the harbor.

The sea was unusually silent, and the speed of the ship suddenly slowed down. The captain stretched out his hand—there was not a single wisp of wind. This was the silence before the storm. He knew: Today he failed to race against the storm. But he did not say anything yet. The black clouds had swallowed all the remaining stars.

The young sailors lying on the deck were also startled by the unusual silence of the sea. They stood up one after another and checked everything on the ship. One person lit a glass ship's lantern, and then there was only one light on the dark sea.

Suddenly, as if being carried on the back of something big, the boat rose high. The sea stood up, and in the dim lamplight, countless huge waves crashed down on the boat like collapsing rocks.

The wind was like a giant swirling, raising the ship with its full sails, constantly moving forward and backward.

At this moment, the rain fell like pouring, hitting his jacket-covered shoulders, making him feel heavy

The captain stood holding the helm. He wanted to break through the storm's encirclement, but he couldn't, the boat just retreated.

"Drop the sails!" So he had to issue such an order. The wind blowing in his face was too strong, and none of the sailors busy with other things heard him.

The boat retreated even faster, "Drop the sails, drop the sails!" He had to shout as hard as he could, but it was still useless. The wind was stronger, the rain was heavier, the ship's lantern was surrounded by a curtain of rain, and he felt the sky was darker standing at the stern of the ship.

The boat kept going backwards, and even in the darkness, the captain knew very clearly that it was about to retreat to a place with reefs. So he resolutely released the rudder, grabbed a kitchen knife, ran to the base of the mast, and desperately chopped at the sail ropes.

The rope broke, and the sail quickly fell, but stopped in the middle. A rope was caught in the pulley. Immediately, one person climbed up like a monkey.

Without securing the rudder, the boat lost control. The wind was spinning, and the boat was spinning too. There was too much rain accumulated on the deck, and the sailors splashed in all directions as they ran. Suddenly, the taut sail and the person who climbed up fell together.

The storm was even more delighted and showing its power, and the boat was tilting left and right. The sailors all knew that they could no longer control the balance of the ship at this time, so they simply sat still.

Suddenly, the captain shouted loudly, another ship was nearby. A little light could be seen through the rain. The pole extending from the stern of the boat had already touched the hull of the other boat. If they retreated again, the two boats would be shattered by the collision.

So all the sailors on both boats were mobilized, desperately pushing each other with poles to keep them at a reasonable distance.

The distance was at most five or six feet, but everyone's shouting sounded like it was half a mile away. In order to make the other party hear clearly, they dragged out each word very long, but the ending was always swallowed by the storm.

The struggle continued for two hours, and the storm finally passed. Then, everyone escaped from the line of death and breathed a long sigh of relief.

The rain was still falling patiently, and the two boats sailed connected towards a familiar harbor. The ship's lantern illuminated the accumulated water on the deck, very brightly.

Someone in the houses next to the small harbor woke up in the middle of the night and heard the happy shouts of several sailors in the gentle sound of the rain.

Ah... Hey!... Ah... Hey!...

Opening Piece "Beautiful Woman Kite"

The climate is fresh in the second month of spring. Celestial winds blow down the sound of emptiness. Looking up into the clouds, there is a ladder to climb. It is only because the east wind is intentionally lifting it up, showing off its talents and standing out from the crowd.

A celestial skirt is left to the swallows. Several elegant performances harmonize with the orioles. I don't know where the Xiao and Yu Sheng flutes are playing. This song is not from heaven. It is like Cai Wenji's Eighteen Songs on the Tartar Pipe, like Xiang Ling drumming the zither with a resounding sound. It is like Zhao Jun's lament on the Pipa, like the talented Red Thread stealing the box lightly. Look at her, with thin sleeves made of plain silk, and clean, light gauze. A pair of jade arms dances with the wind, happily learning the fashionable posture. It is all because of the frivolous and cunning appearance of the rascal boy. Opening Piece "Worn-Out"

Continuous drizzling rain, worn-out dog. Lotus thinking of spring, constantly moving with sorrowful sleep. Orioles and flowers have passed, peach and willow trees are withered. The beginning of summer makes people厌. The beauty is sitting alone in her boudoir, doing needlework, chatting to relieve the worries of her heart. Waiting for her lover to return home early, enjoying the joys of morning and evening like immortals. Most hateful, her lover has been gone for three years without any news. Looking back on the past, it is truly pitiful. Could it be that he has met a prostitute in a foreign land, and his heart has changed in that gentle town? This has caused me to not think about tea or food for three meals a day, and it is difficult to sleep during the long days and short nights. This has caused me to have no heart to do anything during the day, and to guard half a bed alone at night. This has caused me to hang like a bright moon in the sky, with only the shadow of a lonely swallow in front of the window. This has caused me to have muddled thoughts and a disordered mind, and to lie sick for half a year. Fortunately, the divine doctor's holy hand has brought my sick body back to spring and safety. Thinking back, my pair of charming eyes were black and bright, and my face was like a lotus flower. Thinking back, my strands of green silk were like black clouds, but now, it is difficult to manage the bald hair with the bun. Thinking back, my flower-like face and moon-like appearance were plump, but now, I am sallow and skinny in front of the mirror. Thinking back, my figure was slender and healthy, with beautiful curves, but now, I am so thin that I am barely connected. Thinking of the endless sadness, tears fall one after another on my chest. Who will pity my worn-out face?

Shakespeare's Famous Play "As You Like It" Brought to the Screen 219

MGM's "Romeo and Juliet" is about to be released, and another famous Shakespearean play, "As You Like It," has also been brought to the screen, and it is said that it will soon be shown publicly in Shanghai. In these two years, Shakespeare's works seem to be very popular in the film industry. "As You Like It" is a play that starts with tragedy and ends with happiness. Among many of Shakespeare's plays, this is the most lighthearted and fluent, and this film fully preserves the atmosphere of the original work and is performed dramatically. The heroine, Elizabeth Bergner, is the star of the famous film "Catherine the Great." This British actress has performed Shakespearean plays on stage more than six hundred times. Of course, she is more than qualified to play the role of Rosalind in "As You Like It," which is beyond the reach of ordinary American movie stars. All those who love Shakespeare's works, wait for a satisfying enjoyment.

"Forged Love" Scene 220

— Nanjing Ying

Behind the Scenes of "The Rhapsody of United China" 221

In Zhu Shilin's "Ghost", ghostly shadows and sounds appear in the dark room of Li Lili. The setting is eerie and terrifying, and the timid Li Lili cannot help but feel her hair stand on end.

He Mengfu's "Moonlit Night Scene" is co-starred by Li Qing and Zong. It has a superb conception and is full of satire and humor. It can be called a literary work.

Situ Huimin's section "Two Hands of Money" records the waste of the rich, who use two-yuan banknotes as cigarette wrappers, while the poor use them to support the whole family and even cause crime. It contains deep meaning. Starring Mei Jingxi and Lan Ping.

The "Moonlit Night Scene" was composed and scored by the famous musician Sha Mei. It is tragic and desolate, like weeping and complaining.

The Touching "Forged Love" 222

May heaven and earth endure, but this love will know no end.

Shakespeare's great tragedy "Romeo and Juliet" will be given its first Far East honorable screening at the Nanjing Grand Theatre tomorrow night at 9:15 PM. The Chinese translation of the film is "Forged Love." The story in the film is the love story of a pair of young men and women. The meeting of the two at the Ye Yan Ming Lantern, the love words of the two in the Red Window Tower. The frequent singing促, the separation of the two. The ghost made a mistake, and the two drank their hatred and died for love. What is particularly heart-wrenching is the platform love scene. The beauty of the scenery and the moving dialogue in this scene are the crown of the love scenes in each film. The original platform love words written by Shakespeare are widely praised as a famous article in literature. The "Forged Love" filmed by MGM this time, starring Norma Shearer and Leslie Howard, is more beautiful and moving than Shakespeare's original work.
